### [75] [RADAR: Relative Angular Divergence Across Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23028)
*Xavier Cadet,Mateusz Nowak,Peter Chin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为RADAR的新型几何指标，用于预测预训练模型在跨领域迁移时的性能表现。它通过分析模型内部层间的表征轨迹演化，有效识别并规避了潜在的“负迁移”风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器学习实践中，数据获取往往受限或成本高昂。虽然通过增加外部数据源来扩充数据集很常见，但盲目添加数据可能导致“负迁移”（negative transfer），降低模型性能。因此，需要一种能够预先评估不同源域数据对目标域迁移效果的有效指标，以避免性能损失。

Method: 提出了一种名为RADAR的几何导向指标。该方法通过分析模型从层到层的表征演化过程，测量角度对齐情况、层间位移轨迹的相对距离变化，并对比域内与跨域动力学的经验分布差异，从而量化跨领域的可迁移性。

Result: 在跨语言情感分类（文本嵌入模型）和跨领域图像分类（视觉基础模型）等多个基准测试中，RADAR表现出极具竞争力的迁移性预测能力。实验表明，当域转换过程较为平滑或界限清晰时，该指标表现尤为出色。

Conclusion: 本文提出的RADAR指标能够有效度量预训练模型在跨领域迁移时的可迁移性，揭示了模型内部表征空间的几何特征（如层间轨迹的动力学差异）对于迁移表现的关键作用，为预测迁移性能提供了高效的工具。

Abstract: Machine learning methods rely on data. However, gathering suitable data can be challenging due to availability constraints, cost, or the need for domain expertise. Expanding datasets with additional sources is a common response to limited data, yet this practice does not always improve downstream performance and can sometimes lead to a loss of performance, known as negative transfer. We propose RADAR, a simple, geometrically grounded metric for estimating cross-domain transferability in foundation models. RADAR analyzes the layer-wise evolution of representations by measuring angular alignments and relative changes in distance along layer-to-layer displacement trajectories, and by comparing empirical distributions of within-domain and cross-domain dynamics. We hypothesize that domain transferability is related to the divergence between these trajectory distributions. We evaluate the metric across multiple modalities, including cross-lingual sentiment classification with text embedding models and cross-domain image classification with foundation vision models. Across several settings, RADAR provides competitive predictive performance relative to existing transferability metrics on several vision and text benchmarks, with particularly strong results when domain transitions are smooth or cleanly separated. Our ablations further suggest that the effectiveness of transferability estimation depends on the geometry of the model's internal representation space, with different modalities favoring different topological formulations.

### [76] [Uncovering the Latent Potential of Deep Intermediate Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23033)
*Arnesh Batra,Arush Gumber,Aniket Khandelwal,Jashn Khemani,Anubha Gupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对预训练模型深层嵌入信息分布不均的问题，本文提出LOES方法与GeoReg正则化策略，通过精确提取任务判别性子空间并优化表示几何，显著提升了模型迁移学习的效果与可解释性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预训练模型研究多倾向于仅使用最后一层或简单的混合策略，但作者发现任务相关信息在不同层级间是非单调分布的，且无法通过简单的聚合手段完全提取，这限制了模型迁移能力的发挥。

Method: 1. 提出“分层最优嵌入选择”（LOES）：一种通过最小化正交和各向同性约束下的残差误差，来识别任务判别性子空间的构造性谱方法。2. 引入“几何正则化损失”（GeoReg）：通过在微调过程中强制执行类流形的单纯形结构，以稳定表示空间的几何形态。

Result: 在多种架构、深度、模态和数据量级下，LOES方法始终优于标准基线，且随着模型深度的增加，性能增益愈发显著，同时还增强了模型在跨语言和跨模态任务中的可解释性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，预训练模型各层的嵌入几何结构不仅反映了语义信息，更是知识迁移的核心；通过对层间信息分布的深入挖掘，可以显著提升模型在下游任务中的表现，并为跨语言和跨模态的可解释性分析提供了新思路。

Abstract: Foundational Models pretrained on huge amount of data learn representations that evolve across depth, forming a hierarchy of embeddings with distinct semantic content and geometric structure. Contrary to the widespread practice of using only the final layer or shallow mixtures, we show that task-relevant information is distributed non-monotonically across layers and cannot be recovered by naïve aggregation. Through a geometric and empirical study across multiple modalities, we show that effective transfer depends on identifying which layers encode task-discriminative structure and how their embeddings are geometrically organized. We introduce Layer-wise Optimal Embedding Selection (LOES), a constructive spectral method that identifies task-discriminative subspaces by minimizing residual error under orthogonality and isotropy constraints. To align fine-tuning with this selection principle, we further propose Geometric Regularization Loss (GeoReg), which enforces a simplicial structure on class manifolds and stabilizes representation geometry during fine-tuning. Across a wide range of architectures, depths, modalities, and data regimes, LOES consistently outperforms standard baselines, with gains that grow as model depth increases. Beyond accuracy, our method reveals how semantic factors are distributed across layers, thereby enabling cross-lingual and cross-modal interpretability analyses. Together, our results provide strong evidence that layerwise embedding geometry is not incidental but central to how deep models represent and transfer knowledge.

### [78] [Steered Generation via Gradient-Based Optimization on Sparse Query Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23040)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于稀疏自动编码器（SAE）的注意力查询（Query）操控框架，通过解耦和优化查询激活中的稀疏特征，实现了对大语言模型逻辑与风格的精准、可解释控制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Latent steering exploits internal representations of Large Language Models (LLMs) to guide generation, yet interventions on dense states can entangle distinct semantic features. We introduce Prototype-Based Sparse Steering, a framework that applies Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) specifically to query activations, to decompose them into interpretable features, then apply gradient-based optimization during inference to align the sparse representation with class prototypes of target behaviors. ### [79] [Decomposing and Measuring Evaluation Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23055)
*Changling Li,Terry Jingchen Zhang,Jie Zhang,Zhijing Jin,Sahar Abdelnabi,Maksym Andriushchenko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套分析大语言模型“评估意识”的框架，通过 EvalAwareBench 揭示了评估任务的特征如何影响模型行为，发现模型在面对安全评估时表现出更高的敏感度，并强调了增强模型行为一致性对基准测试有效性的重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿语言模型在评估过程中常表现出“评估意识”，即模型意识到自己正在被测试并可能因此调整行为，从而导致基准测试结果偏离真实能力。目前学术界对此缺乏统一的理论框架和度量标准，导致难以区分是测试方法的问题还是模型本身的问题。

Method: 1. 理论建模：借鉴社会心理学，将评估意识分解为“环境因素”（任务可识别性）和“模型因素”（识别能力与行为倾向）。
2. 环境分析：识别出八类触发因素（如占位符、评分格式等），并通过思维链（CoT）监控来探测模型的识别行为。
3. 基准测试：构建 EvalAwareBench，通过控制变量法，在保持核心任务不变的前提下，独立切换八种触发因素，评估九种前沿模型的表现。

Result: 1. 识别率取决于模型与任务的特定组合，而非单一因素。
2. 识别行为不一定会引发表现改变，且改变方向取决于模型对评估类型的感知。
3. 模型对安全评估比能力评估更敏感，导致安全基准测试的有效性风险更高。
4. 没有任何单一触发因素对所有模型产生统一影响，但多个因素叠加会显著增加评估意识。

Conclusion: 评估意识（Evaluation Awareness）是影响模型基准测试有效性的关键因素。该研究强调，评估意识由任务环境特征和模型自身特性共同决定。通过 EvalAwareBench，研究证实评估意识的影响在不同模型和任务间具有高度差异性。未来应关注如何增强模型在识别评估过程中的行为一致性，以确保基准测试的准确度。

Abstract: Frontier language models sometimes recognize that they are being evaluated and adjust their behavior, undermining validity of benchmark results. Yet the field studies it without a shared foundation, conflating properties of the evaluation with properties of the model, and detection with behavioral response. We ground evaluation awareness in social psychology, decomposing it into an environment component (how recognizable the task is) and a model component that separates recognition from propensity to act on it. We operationalize the environment component through eight categorized trigger factors, such as placeholder entities and grading-style output formats, and study recognition and behavior through chain-of-thought monitoring. Across nine frontier models and four benchmarks, recognition rates depend on the specific pairing of model and benchmark rather than on either in isolation. Recognition rarely leads to behavioral change, and when it does, the direction depends on the type of evaluation perceived. Models are also more sensitive to safety than capability evaluations, placing safety benchmark validity at greater risk. To study which factors each model is sensitive to and how they interact, we propose \textbf{EvalAwareBench}, a factor-controlled benchmark of 100 paired safety-capability tasks where each of the eight factors can be independently toggled, varying evaluative signals while holding the underlying request fixed. Through EvalAwareBench, we find that no single factor uniformly affects all models, but stacking factors progressively raises evaluation awareness across all of them. Our framework and EvalAwareBench provide the tools to measure, attribute, and mitigate evaluation awareness, pointing to behavioral consistency under recognition as a promising path forward.

</details>


### [80] [ModeSwitch-LLM: A Lightweight Phase-Aware Controller for Cross-Mode LLM Inference on a Single GPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23057)
*Aman Sunesh,Ali Alshehhi,Hivansh Dhakne*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ModeSwitch-LLM 是一种轻量级推理控制器，通过根据请求特性动态选择最优推理模式（如量化、投机解码等），在保证模型精度的前提下，显著提升了单 GPU 环境下大语言模型的推理速度并大幅降低了能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型推理通常使用单一固定的配置，无法根据不同请求的特性平衡效率、延迟和模型质量。作者旨在通过请求级调度，在单GPU环境下最大化推理效率并降低能耗，同时保持与原始 FP16 推理相当的输出精度。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ModeSwitch-LLM 的轻量级请求边界控制器。该方法利用低成本的工作负载特征，在请求到达时动态路由至最合适的推理模式（如 FP16、量化模式、投机解码或混合模式，如 GPTQ+前缀缓存及 INT8+连续批处理）。研究对比了基于规则的控制器与轻量级学习型路由器的效果。

Result: 在 NVIDIA A100 GPU 上针对 Llama-3.1-8B 模型进行测试，ModeSwitch-LLM 在部署级合成工作负载下，相比 FP16 实现了 2.10 倍的平均延迟加速，能耗降低了 51.7%；同时，模型推理质量保持在极高水平，与 FP16 相比准确度差异仅为 +0.17%。此外，研究发现简单的规则控制器比机器学习模型更具优势，因为它不会带来额外的路由开销，且更符合资源约束。

Conclusion: 通过简单的请求感知路由机制，无需重新训练模型或更改架构，即可在单GPU部署中显著提升大语言模型的推理效率。该研究证明了基于轻量级规则的控制器在平衡延迟、能耗和模型质量方面的有效性，且在大多数场景下优于复杂的机器学习路由方案。

Abstract: ModeSwitch-LLM is a lightweight request-boundary controller for improving single-GPU large language model inference efficiency by routing each request to an appropriate fixed inference mode. Instead of relying on one static serving configuration, the system selects among FP16, quantized modes, speculative decoding, and hybrid modes such as GPTQ plus prefix caching and INT8 plus continuous batching using cheap workload-level features. We evaluate ModeSwitch-LLM on Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct served on a single NVIDIA A100 GPU. On deployment-style synthetic workloads, the online controller achieves a 2.10x mean latency speedup over FP16 and a 0.48x mean energy ratio, corresponding to 51.7% lower energy per token. On automatic benchmarks used as a quality gate, accuracy remains close to FP16 with a mean delta of +0.17 percentage points. We also evaluate lightweight learned routers, but find that they do not clearly outperform the rule-based controller because they add routing overhead and more often select modes that violate quality, energy, or memory constraints. These results show that simple request-aware routing can recover substantial efficiency from existing inference modes without retraining the model or changing its architecture.

### [81] [GEMQ: Global Expert-Level Mixed-Precision Quantization for MoE LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23078)
*Jianing Deng,Song Wang,Dongwei Wang,Zijie Liu,Tianlong Chen,Huanrui Yang,Jingtong Hu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 MoE-LLM 混合精度量化方法通常依赖于层级（Layer-wise）的重要性评估，且忽略了量化导致的路由偏移（Router Shifts）问题，导致模型在内存压缩与精度保持之间无法达到最优平衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GEMQ（全局专家级混合精度量化）的框架，包含两个核心部分：1. 使用全局线性规划（Linear Programming）公式化方法，基于量化误差分析评估全局范围内的专家重要性；2. 引入高效的路由微调机制，使路由策略能够适应量化后的专家。整个过程通过渐进式量化框架进行迭代优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，GEMQ 能够显著降低 MoE 模型的内存占用并加速推理过程，同时将精度损失控制在最小范围内。

Conclusion: GEMQ 证明了通过全局优化和路由微调，可以有效解决专家混合模型（MoE-LLM）在混合精度量化中的重要性评估失真及路由偏移问题，为实现高效能的大模型推理提供了强有力的压缩方案。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts Large Language Models (MoE-LLMs) achieve strong performance but incur substantial memory overhead due to massive expert parameters. Mixed-precision quantization mitigates this cost by allocating expert-wise bit-widths based on their importance, approaching the accuracy-memory Pareto frontier and enabling extreme low-bit quantization. However, existing methods rely on layer-wise importance estimation and overlook router shifts induced by quantization, resulting in suboptimal allocation and routing. In this work, we propose Global Expert-level Mixed-precision Quantization (GEMQ) to overcome these limitations via (1) a global linear-programming formulation that captures model-wide expert importance based on quantization error analysis, and (2) efficient router fine-tuning to adapt routing to quantized experts. These components are integrated into a progressive quantization framework that iteratively refines importance estimation and allocation. Experiments demonstrate that GEMQ significantly reduces memory and accelerates inference with minimal accuracy degradation. Source code is available at https://github.com/jndeng/GEMQ .

</details>


### [82] [The Attribution Contract: Feature Attribution for Generative Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23080)
*Giang Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对生成式语言模型中特征归因定义模糊的问题，提出了“归因契约”框架，主张通过明确归因对象、特征范围及生成假设，解决现有评估方法中的分歧，并强调应将归因方法与契约绑定进行评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的特征归因方法大多源于分类模型，但在生成式语言模型（如自回归模型和扩散模型）中，输入与输出的界限模糊，导致特征的定义不明确。现有的归因研究往往忽略了这种概念上的歧义，导致不同研究者对相同归因方法的解释存在分歧。本文旨在揭示这种概念限制，并建立一套严谨的规范来消除生成模型中归因解释的模糊性。

Method: 本文提出了“归因契约”（Attribution Contract），这是一种规范归因声明的框架。该契约明确了五个核心要素：被解释的输出内容、归因特征的选取范围、假设的生成过程、固定不变的变量以及被归因的模型得分。作者通过自回归模型和扩散模型作为案例研究，对比并分析了在不同生成范式下，针对不同中间状态或生成阶段进行归因的合理性与潜在误导性。

Result: 研究证明，许多关于生成模型特征归因的争论实际上是由于研究者使用了未公开声明的解释契约。通过应用归因契约，研究者可以明确归因方法在何种情况下是信息丰富的，在何种情况下会产生误导。实验表明，归因方法的效果取决于其与特定契约的匹配程度，评估归因方法时应将其视为“方法-契约”对。

Conclusion: 特征归因方法在生成式语言模型中不能脱离特定的解释契约孤立存在。研究指出，生成模型中的归因争议往往源于对解释对象、目标和假设的不一致，因此必须将归因方法与具体的“归因契约”结合起来评估，才能确保归因结果的有效性和可解释性。

Abstract: Feature attribution methods promise to identify which input features matter for a model output. In generative language models, however, it is often unclear what should count as a feature in the first place. In autoregressive language models, earlier generated tokens are both outputs of the model and inputs to later predictions. In diffusion language models, generation proceeds through iterative denoising or unmasking rather than fixed left-to-right prediction, so local explanation may target a state of diffusion rather than a next token. We argue that this ambiguity is not merely an implementation detail, but a conceptual limitation of carrying classifier-era feature attribution directly into generative language modeling. We introduce the Attribution Contract, a specification for feature-attribution claims that names what output is being explained, which features are eligible to receive attribution, what generative process is assumed, what is held fixed, and what model score is being attributed. The contract clarifies why the same attribution method can answer different questions depending on how it is instantiated. We argue that many disagreements about feature attribution in generative language models are not disagreements about attribution algorithms, but about unstated explanatory contracts. Using autoregressive and diffusion language models as case studies, we show when attribution to earlier generated tokens, intermediate states, or denoising stages is informative, when it is misleading, and why feature-attribution methods in generative language models should be evaluated as method-contract pairs.

</details>


### [83] [ThriftAttention: Selective Mixed Precision for Long-Context FP4 Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23081)
*Joe Sharratt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ThriftAttention是一种低位注意力算法，通过仅对极少数（5%）关键查询-键对使用FP16精度，其余采用FP4精度，在保持低位推理高效率的同时，有效解决了长上下文模型量化后的质量退化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的4-bit量化注意力机制在长上下文任务中会导致严重的精度损失，且量化误差在注意力块之间的分布极不均匀，特别是在处理重要Token时误差显著，影响模型整体性能。

Method: 提出了一种两阶段的注意力加速方法：首先，利用启发式算法快速识别出对输出贡献度高的少数查询-键（Query-Key）块；其次，对这些关键块执行FP16运算，其余块保持FP4精度，并通过在线Softmax操作将两条路径的结果合并。

Result: 实验表明，仅需将5%的查询-键块保持在FP16精度，即可恢复平均89.1%的FP4到FP16性能差距，且随着上下文长度增加，该方法的优势愈发明显。

Conclusion: ThriftAttention通过选择性地对关键注意力块使用FP16精度，在维持FP4高效推理的同时，显著解决了长上下文场景下的模型质量下降问题，证明了不均匀的计算精度分配是优化长上下文注意力机制的有效途径。

Abstract: Efficient attention algorithms are critical to mitigate the quadratic cost of attention in long-context workloads. Prior work utilises block-scaled quantisation techniques on Blackwell GPUs to move attention computation to 4-bit precision to accelerate inference. However, these techniques result in significant quality degradation in long-context settings. We show that the output impact of quantisation error is highly non-uniform and increases with the importance of each query-key interaction, concentrating functionally relevant error in a small number of attention blocks that contain the most important tokens. We propose ThriftAttention, a low-bit attention variant that delivers near-FP16 long-context quality at FP4 inference efficiency. This approach proceeds in two stages. First, a heuristic rapidly selects a small number of important query-key block pairs for FP16 precision. Second, the selected blocks are computed in FP16 and the remaining blocks in FP4, with both paths merged via online softmax into a single output. We demonstrate across long-context benchmarks and model families that by computing only 5% of query-key blocks in FP16, ThriftAttention recovers on average 89.1% of the FP4-to-FP16 performance gap. We show ThriftAttention's advantage grows with sequence length, mitigating the systematic FP4 quality degradation observed at longer contexts. The code is available at https://github.com/joesharratt1229/ThriftAttention.

### [84] [Dreaming Smoothly and Sample Efficiently with Gradient Penalized Latent Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23089)

Result: 实验表明，GPLD在DeepMind Control套件的本体感知任务中提升了整体样本效率，特别是在高复杂度运动环境中表现突出。在更具挑战性的四足机器人任务中，GPLD不仅能更快达到高回报水平，且在长视界内的后期学习中表现出更好的一致性。

Conclusion: 显式的局部平滑正则化是一种简单且有效的方法，可以增强潜空间世界模型在连续控制环境中的表现。GPLD通过利用这一归纳偏置，显著提升了模型的学习效率和稳定性。

Abstract: Model-based reinforcement learning improves sample efficiency by learning a world model. However, existing latent world models such as DreamerV3 do not explicitly enforce local smoothness in their learned transition dynamics, leaving a useful inductive bias for transition dynamics learning unexploited. We propose GPLD, a gradient-penalized latent dynamics regularizer for DreamerV3 that applies a row-wise Jacobian penalty to the posterior latent distribution to encourage locally smooth transition learning. We show that this penalty can be interpreted as the continuous-latent analog of finite-difference smoothing of transition laws in discrete embedded-state MDPs, and estimate it efficiently using Hutchinson-style stochastic probes. Empirically, across DeepMind Control proprioceptive tasks, GPLD improves aggregate sample efficiency, with particularly strong gains on higher-complexity locomotion environments. On more challenging quadruped tasks, GPLD reaches high-return behavior earlier and exhibits more consistent late-stage learning over longer horizons. Explicit local smoothness regularization is a simple and effective way to improve latent world models for smooth continuous control environments. Code for GPLD is available at github.com/romils9/gpld-mbrl .

### [85] [Robust OT-Guided Generative Residual Domain Adaptation for Bike-Sharing Demand Prediction under Temporal Domain Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23115)

Abstract: Bike-sharing models trained on historical station-hour data may degrade when deployed in later years because travel patterns change over time. This paper studies March Citi Bike demand prediction from 2021 to 2026 as a temporal domain adaptation problem and proposes Gen-ROTDA, a robust optimal transport-guided residual domain adaptation framework. The method fits a target-domain station-time anchor with a small labeled target subset, transfers residual rather than raw demand, applies a deterministic label-preserving residual feature generator, and trims high-cost transport matches before training the final residual predictor. Experiments compare Gen-ROTDA with anchor-only, source-only, target-only, fine-tuning, MMD adaptation, Sinkhorn OTDA, ROTDA, and Gen-OTDA. Gen-ROTDA achieves the lowest MAE on the main 2025 to 2026 task and is the best OT-family method on average across multi-year tasks, although fine-tuning and MMD adaptation remain strong overall baselines. Under abnormal target-unlabeled records, Gen-ROTDA is much more stable than non-robust OT variants, suggesting that robust transport is useful for noisy temporal transfer in bike-sharing demand prediction.

### [86] [When Do LLMs Reason? A Dynamical Systems View via Entropy Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22873)
*Wei Xia,Haoqing Wang,Zhi-Hong Deng,Yehui Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对思维链（CoT）在非复杂任务中浪费资源的矛盾，本文提出了EDRM框架，利用解码早期的熵动态特征实时判断是否需要执行思维链，实现了高效、自适应的推理调度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究发现思维链（CoT）虽能增强推理能力，但在事实性及开放式任务中往往导致计算资源浪费且收益微弱甚至负面。作者旨在解决何时启用显式推理这一关键问题，探索推理行为在解码过程中的动态演化规律。

Method: 提出了基于熵动力学的推理流形（EDRM）框架。该方法通过监测大模型在推理早期生成的熵轨迹，将其映射到低维流形空间，并以此作为信号，动态决策是否需要启用思维链（CoT）推理，实现了轻量级且无需训练的实例级推理策略路由。

Result: 在15个基准测试和4种不同规模模型上的实验表明，EDRM在数据集层面实现了41%–55%的Token节省并提升了准确率；在实例层面，在保持27%–45%节省的同时，准确率最高提升了4.7%。该框架仅需少量校准样本即可部署，表现优于静态基准方法。

Conclusion: 推理不应作为大模型的默认策略，而应根据任务需求进行选择性调用。该研究证明了基于早期解码熵的自适应推理控制机制能够显著提升推理效率，并在保证或提升准确率的同时大幅降低计算成本。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has become the default strategy for enhancing LLM capabilities, yet its application raises a fundamental question: when is explicit reasoning actually beneficial? Empirical evidence reveals a striking paradox: CoT often provides marginal or even negative gains on factual and open-ended tasks while multiplying token consumption. In this work, we show that LLM reasoning is not a static property of tasks or models, but a \emph{dynamic decoding state} that emerges during generation. Through systematic analysis, we find early-stage entropy dynamics provide a reliable signal of this state: tasks benefiting from CoT exhibit consistent entropy reduction, while others display unstable or increasing patterns. This behavior can be interpreted as a phase-transition-like shift from a high-entropy exploratory regime to a low-entropy structured reasoning regime. Based on these insights, we propose \textbf{EDRM} (Entropy Dynamics-based Reasoning Manifold), a lightweight and training-free routing framework that leverages early decoding entropy to adaptively select inference strategies. EDRM embeds entropy trajectories into a compact and interpretable manifold representation, enabling both zero-shot deployment and fine-grained instance-level adaptation. Across 15 benchmarks and 4 LLMs of varying scales and architectures, EDRM consistently outperforms static baselines. At the dataset level, EDRM achieves \textbf{41--55\%} token reduction while improving accuracy with as few as 50 calibration samples. At the instance level, it further improves accuracy by up to \textbf{4.7\%} while maintaining \textbf{27--45\%} token savings. These results suggest that reasoning should be invoked selectively rather than by default, and demonstrate the effectiveness of entropy-driven decoding control for efficient and adaptive LLM inference.

### [87] [When Determinants Are Not Enough: Private Rare Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23131)
*Xingyu Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于广义瑞利商的稀疏切换规则，解决了差分隐私线性强化学习中因噪声导致设计矩阵单调性失效的问题，有效恢复了策略更新的理论性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线性多臂老虎机（Linear Bandits）和强化学习中，标准的基于行列式的更新规则依赖于设计矩阵的单调性。然而，在引入差分隐私所需的加性高斯噪声后，设计矩阵的单调性不再成立，导致现有的遗憾分析（regret analysis）框架失效，因此需要一种新的策略来恢复分析的有效性。

Method: 引入了一种基于广义瑞利商（Generalized Rayleigh quotient）的稀疏切换（rare-switching）规则。该方法替代了标准的行列式更新规则，通过在差分隐私约束下，重新建立置信宽度（confidence-width）的比较逻辑，从而恢复了对数级别的策略更新效率。

Result: 通过该方法，成功恢复了在差分隐私环境下对数级别的策略更新频率，并证明了在常数因子内满足所需的置信宽度界限，从而保证了算法的收敛性和性能。

Conclusion: 作者通过与Codex的协作，成功解决并证明了在差分隐私线性强化学习中，由于高斯噪声引入导致设计矩阵单调性丧失从而使得常规分析失效的问题。该研究展示了利用广义瑞利商构建稀疏切换规则的有效性，为差分隐私环境下的策略更新提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this note, I would like to share a small research moment where Codex helped me find the right way to adapt rare switching to the private setting. The standard determinant-based update rule in linear bandits and RL works beautifully because the design matrix grows monotonically. But once Gaussian noise is added for privacy, this monotonicity can fail, and the usual analysis no longer goes through. The key reason is that determinant growth controls volume, while regret analysis needs control of the worst direction. To address this, Codex comes up with a different rare-switching rule based on the generalized Rayleigh quotient, which restores logarithmic policy updates and the desired confidence-width comparison up to a constant factor. I present my manually clean-up version of the proof here as well as some personal reflection on this example.

### [88] [Tensor Cache: Eviction-conditioned Associative Memory for Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22884)
*Kabir Swain,Sijie Han,Daniel Karl I. Weidele,Mauro Martino,Antonio Torralba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Tensor Cache 是一种通过外积存储机制增强滑动窗口注意力的两级缓存技术，在限制内存占用的前提下，有效解决了长文本推理中历史信息丢失的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归 Transformer 的 KV 缓存随上下文长度线性增长，内存压力巨大。现有的滑动窗口技术虽然限制了内存使用，但会导致被淘汰的旧信息永久丢失。该研究旨在设计一种既能保持固定内存开销，又能有效留存长程上下文信息的缓存方案，以突破上下文长度与内存利用率之间的瓶颈。

Method: 引入 Tensor Cache 两级缓存机制：第一级（L1）为标准的滑动窗口注意力，处理近期 token；第二级（L2）为外积快速权重存储，用于捕捉被 L1 淘汰的 KV 对。利用线性注意力恒等式（Linear Attention Identity），通过矩阵乘法从 L2 检索信息。此外，通过修正分块训练中的偏差，采用并行加权扫描（parallel weighted-sum scan）精确实现了逐 token 更新，并端到端训练门控机制及衰减参数。

Result: 实验表明，Tensor Cache 在系统扩展性、关联性回忆、长文本语言建模及内存容量诊断等测试中，均优于现有的受限状态（bounded-state）基准模型，在内存消耗与模型性能之间达到了更优的平衡。

Conclusion: Tensor Cache 成功打破了滑动窗口注意力机制在长上下文任务中的性能上限。通过将外积存储作为二级缓存，该方法在保持固定内存占用的同时，显著提升了模型对长距离上下文信息的提取能力，是实现高效、可扩展的长文本建模的有效路径。

Abstract: Autoregressive Transformer KV caches grow linearly with context length; sliding-window caching bounds memory but discards evicted tokens entirely, so relevant evidence outside the window becomes inaccessible. We introduce \emph{Tensor Cache}, a two-level cache that pairs sliding-window softmax attention as a first-level cache (L1) with a fixed-size outer-product fast-weight memory as a second-level cache (L2) fed by KV pairs evicted from the window. Recent tokens remain in exact local attention; evicted pairs are compressed into a per-layer matrix $A$ and read by future queries through a single matrix multiplication, exploiting the linear-attention identity $q_t(k_i \otimes v_i)=\langle q_t,k_i\rangle v_i$. A learned scalar gate fuses the L1 and L2 outputs, and per-head decay and write-rate parameters are trained end-to-end. The outer-product memory and the read identity are well-known; our contribution is their use as an L2 cache fed exclusively by sliding-window evictions, plus identifying that the common chunked-mean training shortcut $A\!\leftarrow\!λA\!+\!η(\bar k\!\otimes\!\bar v)$ silently introduces $C^2{-}C$ spurious cross-token outer products per chunk, and closing the gap with a parallel weighted-sum scan equivalent to per-token writes within float32 epsilon. Across systems scaling, controlled associative recall, long-context language modeling, and memory-capacity diagnostics, Tensor Cache improves the memory--quality frontier over bounded-state baselines.

</details>


### [89] [CALAD: Channel-Aware contrastive Learning for multivariate time series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23139)
*Jaehyeop Hong,Youngbum Hur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CALAD 是一种针对多变量时间序列的通道感知对比学习框架，它通过评估各通道对异常检测的贡献度，引导模型重点关注关键通道，从而提升了在标签稀缺及分布偏移场景下的异常检测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多变量时间序列异常检测方法多采用无监督学习，但往往将所有通道同等对待，导致异常相关的关键信号被无关噪声淹没。为了解决这一问题，本文旨在引入一种能区分通道重要性并聚焦于异常语义的特征学习机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CALAD 的通道感知对比学习框架。该方法首先利用基于 Transformer 的自编码器计算重构误差以评估各通道的相关性，进而根据相关性设计了通道级的增强策略。在对比学习过程中，通过对异常相关通道进行扰动或保持来构建正负样本，并结合辅助重构任务共同训练，使模型同时具备判别性表征学习和正常数据结构建模的能力。

Result: 在多个真实数据集上的实验结果表明，CALAD 在异常检测性能上持续优于现有的先进方法，尤其在处理数据分布发生偏移的情况下，表现出了更强的适应性和检测稳定性。

Conclusion: CALAD 通过引入通道相关性引导的对比学习，有效解决了多变量时间序列中不同通道贡献度不均的问题，在保持正常模式重构能力的同时，显著提升了对异常语义的捕捉能力，特别是在分布偏移场景下表现出优异的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Multivariate time series anomaly detection has become increasingly important in real-world applications, where labeled data are often scarce. Many existing approaches rely on unsupervised learning to model normal patterns, but they often treat all channels equally. This design can dilute anomaly-relevant signals, since not all channels contribute equally to anomaly detection. In this paper, we propose CALAD, a channel-aware contrastive learning framework for multivariate time series anomaly detection. CALAD governs the construction of contrastive samples using estimated channel relevance, allowing the learning process to reflect anomaly semantics rather than generic similarity. Channel relevance is estimated from reconstruction errors of a transformer-based autoencoder and is used to distinguish channels that are more influential to anomalous behaviors. Using this information, we design a channel-wise augmentation strategy in which positive and negative samples are constructed based on whether anomaly-relevant channels are preserved or perturbed. This encourages invariance to changes in irrelevant channels while being sensitive to changes in anomaly-relevant channels. Furthermore, CALAD combines contrastive learning and an auxiliary reconstruction head, allowing the model to learn discriminative representations while retaining normal structures. Experiments on multiple real-world datasets shows that CALAD consistently outperforms existing methods, particularly under distribution shift scenarios. We provide the code for reproducibility at https://github.com/hirundo1218/CALAD

### [90] [Infra-Bayesian Reinforcement Learning Agents Outperform Classical RL For Worst-Case Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23146)
*Manish Aryal,Faiyaz Azam,Agnivo Banerjee,Sai Sidhanth Manoharan Jayanthi,Allegra Laro,Clément Legentilhomme,Andrew Lin,Florian Lorkowski,Radman Rakhshandehroo,Patric Rommel,Emanuel Ruzak,Nathan Theng,Paul Yushin Rapoport*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“基础贝叶斯强化学习”框架，通过从“最大化平均预期”转向“最大化最坏情况预期”，解决了传统强化学习在模型错误设定及对抗性环境下的鲁棒性缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强化学习基于“可实现性”（realizability）假设，即环境行为不依赖于智能体的策略。但在现实的AI安全场景（如与预测器、人类或其他智能体交互）中，该假设失效，模型 misspecification（错误设定）会导致经典贝叶斯方法产生极度自信但错误的后验估计，导致决策失败和不可控的后悔值。为了解决这种“奈特式不确定性”，需要一种能够处理模型偏差的鲁棒决策框架。

Method: 提出了一种“基础贝叶斯”强化学习框架，利用“基础贝叶斯条件更新”（Infra-Bayesian conditioning）维护一组不精确的假设集合，并采用“最大最小化”（maximin）策略，即在面对模型不确定性时，始终选择最坏情况下的最优动作，而非简单的加权平均。

Result: 在存在奈特式不确定性的模拟环境中，基础贝叶斯智能体展现出了比传统强化学习智能体更低的“最坏情况后悔值”（worst-case regret）；在纽科姆悖论（Newcomb's problem）中，该智能体能够识别并选择最优策略，表现优于传统决策理论智能体。

Conclusion: 该研究通过在有限状态决策问题中实现“基础贝叶斯”（Infra-Bayesian）强化学习，证明了在模型错误设定和存在奈特式不确定性（Knightian uncertainty）的环境下，通过最大化最坏情况预期价值的决策策略，能够有效提高AI系统的鲁棒性和决策可靠性，是解决非可实现环境下AI安全问题的关键一步。

Abstract: Classical reinforcement learning assumes the agent interacts with a fixed environment whose behavior does not depend on the agent's policy. This assumption breaks down in non-realizable settings where other actors might anticipate the agent's behavior, including environments crucial to AI safety, where the agent interacts with predictors, humans, other AI agents, and institutions. In such settings, the agent's model class fails to capture the world in which it operates. Under such misspecification, classical Bayesian methods can produce confidently wrong posteriors, unreliable decisions, and unbounded regret, as realizability fails to obtain. Infra-Bayesianism is a decision-theoretic framework that addresses these failures by distinguishing ordinary probabilistic uncertainty, where priors can be reasonably chosen, from Knightian uncertainty, where no grounds exist for the construction of such a prior. It does so by evaluating actions on their worst-case outcomes, rather than from posterior expectations or weighted averaging. We present the first proof-of-concept implementation of an infra-Bayesian reinforcement learning architecture for finite-outcome stateless decision problems. Our agent maintains a set of imprecise hypotheses, updates them using infra-Bayesian conditioning, and selects actions by maximizing worst-case expected value. We apply this implementation of the infra-Bayesian maximin decision process to an environment with Knightian uncertainty, and demonstrate a lower worst-case regret as compared to classical reinforcement learning agents. We also investigate Newcomb's problem and show that the infra-Bayesian agent picks the optimal strategy, outperforming classical decision theory agents. Our results provide a step towards reinforcement learning agents that remain robust under model misspecification and policy-dependent uncertainty.

</details>

Abstract: Recent advancements in instructional fine-tuning have injected noise into embeddings, with NEFTune (Jain et al., 2024) setting benchmarks using uniform noise. Despite NEFTune's empirical findings that uniform noise outperforms Gaussian noise, the reasons for this remain unclear. This paper aims to clarify this by offering a thorough analysis, both theoretical and empirical, indicating comparable performance among these noise types. Additionally, we introduce a new fine-tuning method for language models, utilizing symmetric noise in embeddings. This method aims to enhance the model's function by more stringently regulating its local curvature, demonstrating superior performance over the current method, NEFTune. When fine-tuning the LLaMA-2-7B model using Alpaca, standard techniques yield a 29.79% score on AlpacaEval. However, our approach, SymNoise, increases this score significantly to 69.04%, using symmetric noisy embeddings. This is a 6.7% improvement over the state-of-the-art method, NEFTune (64.69%). Furthermore, when tested on various models and stronger baseline instruction datasets, such as Evol-Instruct, ShareGPT, OpenPlatypus, SymNoise consistently outperforms NEFTune. The current literature, including NEFTune, has underscored the importance of more in-depth research into the application of noise-based strategies in the fine-tuning of language models. Our approach, SymNoise, is another significant step towards this direction, showing notable improvement over the existing state-of-the-art method.

### [92] [Pure Exploration for a Good Policy in Reinforcement Learning with Bandit Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23182)
*Zitian Li,Wang Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对强化学习中对最优策略识别（BPI）的需求过高问题，本文提出了“良好策略识别（GPI）”框架，并设计了BEE-GPI算法。该算法能够高效识别达到指定阈值的策略，其采样复杂度不再受限于状态动作空间大小，仅取决于奖励阈值与最优值之间的差距，具有更高的实际应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习纯探索研究多集中在最佳策略识别（BPI）上，但在实际应用中，往往只需找到一个“足够好”的策略即可，无需追求全局最优。为了解决这一更具实际意义的问题，作者提出了良好策略识别（GPI）框架。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为BEE-GPI的算法。该算法在固定置信度设置下运行，通过迭代采样来评估策略表现，并在满足给定阈值μ₀时输出结果或判定不存在该类策略。算法利用了阈值限制来优化探索效率，避开了对全局最优策略的精确估计。

Result: 理论分析表明，BEE-GPI算法的采样复杂度上界在正例情况下包含O(H²/(V*-μ₀)²)，其中H为片段长度，V*为最优期望奖励。该结果表明复杂度不直接依赖于状态和动作空间的大小。此外，下界分析证明了该算法在渐进意义上的最优性。数值实验进一步证实了该方法的高效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的BEE-GPI算法在良好策略识别（GPI）任务中实现了理论上的最优采样复杂度。GPI比传统的最佳策略识别（BPI）更具灵活性和实用性，尤其是在对策略性能有明确阈值要求的情境下，显著降低了探索成本。

Abstract: Pure exploration in episodic Reinforcement Learning has primarily focused on Best Policy Identification (BPI), which seeks to identify a (near)-optimal policy with high confidence. Motivated by practical settings where a ``good enough'' policy suffices, we study an alternate objective of Good Policy Identification (GPI). For a given reward threshold $μ_0$, GPI only requires identifying a policy with expected reward in an episode at least $μ_0$ if such a policy exists (positive instance), or declaring None if no such policy exists (negative instance). We formalize GPI under the fixed-confidence setting. We require the output to be correct with probability $\geq 1-δ$, and seek to minimize the expected sample complexity, which is the expected number of episodes explored for the output. We propose a novel algorithm BEE-GPI, and derive theoretically-grounded upper bounds on its sample complexity for positive and negative instances. Notably, for positive instances, the coefficient of $\log 1/δ$ in our upper bound is $O(H^2/(V^* - μ_0)^2)$, where $H$ is the episode length and $V^*$ is the optimal expected reward in an episode. The coefficient does not depend on the action and state space sizes otherwise, in sharp contrast to the sample complexity in BPI. We further establish lower bound results to show the near-optimality of BEE-GPI and the necessity of the $1/(V^* -μ)^2$ term. Numerical experiments further validate the efficiency of our approach.

</details>


### [93] [Empirical Bayes Conformal Prediction for Vision and Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23189)
*Jiapeng Zeng,Yogesh Prabhu,Zhanpeng Zeng,Michael A. Newton,Vikas Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用“r-value”的经验贝叶斯共形预测框架，通过量化模型评分的不确定性来区分稳定信号与噪声，从而在保证覆盖率的前提下，显著提升了现代视觉和语言模型预测的稳定性和准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的共形预测通常依赖于单一的、不稳定的非一致性分数，这会导致仅仅因为某次采样或提示词（prompt）偶然产生的高分，使得不稳定的预测被错误地包含在共形集合中。作者旨在利用分数的不确定性（变异性）来区分稳定的信号与噪声，从而改善预测结果的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了一种基于经验贝叶斯（Empirical Bayes）的共形预测框架，通过r-value将分数的变异性转化为信息丰富的非一致性分数（nonconformity score）。该方法支持闭式正态-正态经验贝叶斯估计器和非参数后验采样估计器，并利用分数的均值与其不确定性来重新评估候选者的排名。

Result: 在图像分类、基于CLIP的视觉语言模型（VLM）及大语言模型（LLM）等基准测试中，基于r-value的共形预测在保持预设覆盖率的同时，有效降低了高方差假阳性样本的纳入率，提升了排序稳定性，并减小了预测集的大小。

Conclusion: 通过引入r-value，该研究展示了在共形预测中利用分数的变异性（即不确定性）不仅能保持目标覆盖率，还能显著提升预测集合的稳定性和缩减集合规模，特别是在模型输出存在波动的情况下。r-value提供了一种有效衡量模型预测“潜在稳定性”的方法。

Abstract: Conformal prediction (CP) gives distribution-free coverage for modern vision and language models, but it is often forced to make a ranking decision from a single unstable nonconformity score. Standard CP uses one realization, while average-then-calibrate variants smooth multiple realizations into a point estimate. Both options discard the inconsistency that can help identify whether a candidate is indeed stable. A weak answer can enter the conformal set even if the evidence is not strong, simply because one posterior sample or prompt phrasing made it look strong. But variability can help distinguish a stable signal from noise-driven fluctuations. We describe an empirical Bayes conformal prediction framework that uses $r$-values to convert score variability into an uncertainty informed nonconformity score. The resulting $r$-value estimates how likely a candidate's latent score belongs to the top-ranked group after accounting for both its mean score and its uncertainty. It admits both a closed-form Normal-Normal empirical Bayes estimator and a nonparametric posterior-sampling estimator. Using the $r$-value as the nonconformity score preserves the target conformal coverage while provably reducing the inclusion of high variance false candidates under mild regularity conditions. Across image classification, CLIP-based VLM benchmarks, and LLMs, we show that $r$-value conformal prediction preserves target coverage while improving ranking stability and reducing set size when variability is informative, and reverting to CP-like behavior when variability vanishes.

### [94] [Expand More, Shrink Less: Shaping Effective-Rank Dynamics for Dense Scaling in Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23191)
*Guoming Li,Shangyu Zhang,Junwei Pan,Wentao Ning,Jin Chen,Gengsheng Xue,Chao Zhou,Shudong Huang,Haijie Gu,Menglin Yang*

Abstract: Scaling recommendation models is a central challenge in recommender systems. Recently, RankMixer has emerged as an effective solution, operating on a unified token representation and alternating between token mixing and per-token feedforward networks (P-FFNs) to achieve scalable performance. However, RankMixer suffers from \textit{embedding collapse}, where learned representations have low effective rank, limiting expressivity and underutilizing the expanded representation space. Through empirical analysis and theoretical insights, we identify rigid token mixing and P-FFN modules as the primary causes of this phenomenon, jointly inducing a \textbf{damped oscillatory trajectory} in effective-rank evolution across layers. To address it, we propose RankElastor, a novel architecture that produces spectrum-robust representations with provable collapse mitigation. RankElastor introduces two components: (i) \textbf{parameterized full mixing}, which enables expressive token mixing with improved spectral robustness; and (ii) \textbf{GLU-improved P-FFNs}, which stabilize representation spectra through GLU-style FFN modules. Extensive experiments on large-scale industrial datasets demonstrate that RankElastor consistently improves recommendation performance, mitigates embedding collapse, and exhibits robust scaling behavior. Code is available at this GitHub repository: https://github.com/vasile-paskardlgm/RankElastor

Abstract: Dataset pruning reduces the storage and training costs of deep learning by selecting an informative subset from a large dataset. Recent label-free pruning methods address this issue, but they rely on features from pretrained models to estimate example difficulty. This dependence can be unreliable when the target dataset differs substantially from the pretraining distribution. We propose SemiPrune, a label-efficient dataset pruning framework, using only a small randomly labeled subset, that uses semi-supervised learning to generate pseudo-labels for unlabeled data, allowing existing supervised pruning methods that require label information to be seamlessly applied to the resulting pseudo-labeled training pool. We then estimate example difficulty from pseudo-label-induced training dynamics and select a coreset. ### [96] [PaP-NF: Probabilistic Long-Term Time Series Forecasting via Prefix-as-Prompt Reprogramming and Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23219)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时间序列预测模型大多依赖于确定性预测，难以应对现实世界中复杂的环境不确定性。为了能够量化并表示预测中的不确定性，需要开发有效的概率预测方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 PaP-NF 的概率预测框架。该方法利用 Prefix-as-Prompt 机制将连续时间序列表示与冻结的大语言模型（LLM）对齐，并使用基于 LLM 提取的全局上下文来条件化一个归一化流（Normalizing Flow）解码器，从而输出预测分布。

Result: 在多个长期预测基准测试中，PaP-NF 能够稳健地捕捉多模态不确定性，同时保持了具有竞争力的点预测精度（通过 CRPS 指标评估）。

Conclusion: PaP-NF 通过结合冻结的大语言模型和归一化流，证明了利用大型预训练模型捕捉时间序列的不确定性是高效且有效的，为 probabilistic forecasting 提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Time series forecasting plays a central role in many real-world applications and has been extensively studied. Most existing approaches rely on deterministic models. However, real-world environments exhibit inherently uncertain and complex future behaviors, making single-point predictions insufficient. This highlights the need for probabilistic forecasting methods that can quantify and represent uncertainty. In this work, we propose PaP-NF, a probabilistic forecasting framework that aligns continuous time series representations with a frozen large language model (LLM) using a Prefix-as-Prompt mechanism, and conditions a normalizing flow decoder on the global context extracted by the LLM. The quality of the resulting predictive distributions is evaluated using the Continuous Ranked Probability Score (CRPS), a standard metric in probabilistic forecasting. Across a variety of long-term forecasting benchmarks, PaP-NF robustly captures multi-modal uncertainty while maintaining competitive point forecasting accuracy. The official implementation is available at: https://github.com/democracy04/PaP-NF

Method: 提出了一种基于移动模式的空间公平性评估方法：首先将个体的移动轨迹映射到不同分辨率和对齐方式的空间分区中，随后利用空间扫描统计量（spatial scan statistic）来检测预测模型在不同移动模式下是否存在不公平惩罚，并量化该不公平性。

Abstract: Assessing the spatial fairness of predictive models involves establishing whether they are statistically penalizing (favoring) individuals associated with certain geographical locations. Literature on this topic makes the fundamental assumption that each individual is assigned to a single geographical location (e.g., place of residence). However, fairness with respect to the set of locations where one has been, i.e., their movement patterns over different regions, also matters when fairness is considered. Consequently, we argue that it is necessary to generalize the notion of spatial fairness to also include movement patterns, leading to the novel problem of assessing predictive models for fairness relative to the movements of individuals. To deal with this problem, we propose an approach that first associates the movements of individuals to certain geographic regions, considering multiple spatial partitions with different resolutions and alignments, and then employs a suitable spatial scan statistic to assess whether a predictive model is fair based on movement patterns. In the experimental evaluation, we study the performance of our approach over thousands of synthetic unfair datasets, showing that it is effective at detecting this new type of unfairness and at retrieving the set of objects treated unfairly, while localization performance exhibits a consistent multi-resolution trade-off.

We propose Convex Language Detection (CLD), a novel framework that integrates theoretically grounded convex optimization techniques into the spoken dialogue systems pipeline. Our method is efficiently implemented via multi-GPU Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM) in JAX, thus providing global optimality guarantees and fast training in polynomial time. Method: 提出 RelPrism 框架：1. 构建多维度（内在、关系、混合）属性；2. 对每个维度应用多粒度聚类以形成伪任务池；3. 通过在这些多维、多粒度任务池上进行预训练，强制模型学习更全面的数据表示。

Abstract: Relational databases (RDBs) remain the cornerstone of modern data systems and support diverse predictive tasks. Recent relational deep learning (RDL) methods enable end-to-end prediction by converting RDBs into graphs, where rows are represented as nodes and inter-table interactions are represented as edges, and then applying graph-based models for representation learning. Despite the strong capability of RDL, effective self-supervised pre-training for RDBs remains non-trivial. RDB tasks often require multi-faceted information across different perspectives and granularities. For example, user churn classification may rely more on interaction patterns, whereas consumption value prediction requires both user-item behaviors and intrinsic user attributes for fine-grained regression. Such heterogeneous needs challenge RDB representation learning, as pre-training objectives should cover comprehensive information for downstream adaptation. However, existing SSL methods typically derive supervision from a single facet, such as node-level intrinsic attributes or subgraph-level relational structures, providing limited adaptability. To this end, we propose RelPrism, a multi-faceted self-supervised learning framework for RDBs. RelPrism constructs intrinsic, relational, and hybrid attributes from distinct perspectives, and applies multi-granularity clustering to each perspective to form corresponding pseudo-task pools. Pre-training over these pools exposes representations to broader perspectives and granularity levels, yielding a stronger basis for downstream adaptation. Experiments on 14 tasks across 5 real-world datasets show that RelPrism improves ROC-AUC by 4.15% for classification and reduces MAE by 10.75% for regression over state-of-the-art baselines. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/RelPrism.

Abstract: Learning-augmented algorithms have emerged as a powerful paradigm to surpass traditional worst-case lower bounds by integrating potentially noisy predictions. We provide the first systematic study of learning-augmented scheduling that curbs preemption while optimizing latency. We establish that the gap between theoretical latency bounds and preemption overhead can be bridged with solid analytical foundations. Our results include $O(1)$-competitive algorithms for single and unrelated parallel machines with only $O(1)$ preemptions per job under accurate predictions, with overhead scaling logarithmically with the prediction error. Method: 提出了一种名为 VECTOR 的即插即用型增强方法，通过三元路由策略处理 KV Cache：(1) 保留关键标记；(2) 对可重构标记进行近似处理；(3) 丢弃冗余标记。该方法结合了基础评分器的重要性信号与离线校准的回归价值评估模型，以量化标记的可重构性。

Existing methods are often dominated by binary eviction or representation approximation, which may underutilize tokens that are not critical for exact retention but are still reconstructable. We present VECTOR, a plug-and-play augmentation for eviction-based pipelines that introduces three-way token routing: retention, approximation, and eviction. VECTOR combines an importance signal from the base scorer with a reconstructability signal from an offline-calibrated regression-based value estimation. By leveraging reconstructability, VECTOR recovers useful value information that would otherwise be irreversibly lost under binary eviction, while preserving key vectors for attention routing stability. Experimental results show that VECTOR improves quality-memory trade-offs under medium-to-high compression, with especially clear gains in stricter budget regimes.

### [102] [When Good Equations Get Bad Scores: Improving Symbolic Regression Through Better Parameter Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23272)
*Boxiao Wang,Kai Li,Zhiwei Chen,Yang Huang,Runxiang Wang,Ziwen Zhang,Yifan Zhang,Jian Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对符号回归中因参数拟合不佳导致“好结构被错误低估”的问题，本文提出了 SAGE-Fit 框架，通过引入结构与语义先验来优化内层拟合，从而大幅提升搜索效率与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的符号回归方法普遍采用双层优化框架，其中内层的参数拟合直接影响外层的搜索。由于非线性算子的存在，内层优化往往陷入局部最优，导致正确的公式结构因为参数拟合不佳而获得低分，从而误导搜索过程。这种“结构好但评分差”的现象是制约符号回归效率和准确性的核心瓶颈。

Method: 提出了 SAGE-Fit 框架。该方法利用符号回归（SR）中表达式固有的双重原生先验：结构先验和语义先验，为每种特性设计了专门的优化模块，以改善非线性拟合中的非凸优化问题，避免因局部最优导致的错误评分。

Result: 实验表明，SAGE-Fit 作为一种即插即用的模块，能够显著提高符号回归的评估保真度，并能在各种主流的符号回归系统中实现性能的普遍提升。

Conclusion: SAGE-Fit 通过利用符号表达式特有的结构和语义先验，有效地解决了符号回归中“结构好但评分差”的优化瓶颈，为提升现有符号回归系统的评估准确性和整体搜索性能提供了一个即插即用的通用方案。

Abstract: Symbolic Regression (SR) plays a central role in scientific knowledge discovery by distilling mathematical equations from observational data. Most existing SR methods function within a bi-level optimization framework: an outer loop that searches for the discrete equation structure, and an inner loop that optimizes the continuous parameters of that structure. Crucially, parameter-fitting quality directly determines a structure's score and thus the outer-loop search. However, nonlinear operators make the inner loop highly non-convex, and budget-driven reliance on fast local solvers (e.g., BFGS) often yields poor local minima and underestimated scores for correct structures. This ``Good Structure, Bad Score'' phenomenon becomes a key bottleneck, degrading efficiency and misguiding the search away from the true equation. To resolve this, we propose SAGE-Fit (Structure-Aware and Semantics-Guided Evaluator for Symbolic Regression), an SR-native fitting framework that exploits the dual native priors of symbolic expressions. By capitalizing on the structural and semantic priors unique to SR, we design tailored modules for each property, thereby effectively mitigating this optimization bottleneck. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach, as a plug-and-play module, significantly enhances evaluation fidelity and universally improves the performance of various SR systems.

### [103] [Prudent-Banker: No Extra Fees for Baseline Safety in Adversarial Bandits With and Without Delays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23351)
*Ting Hu,Luanda Cai,Emmanouil-Vasileios Vlatakis-Gkaragkounis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Prudent-Banker 算法，解决了延迟反馈下对抗性多臂老虎机在追求最优性能的同时如何保持安全性的难题，实现了理论上的最优权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在延迟反馈的对抗性多臂老虎机问题中，现有的算法难以平衡“实现极小极大最优后悔值”与“维持对安全基准策略的近恒定后悔值”之间的矛盾。任意延迟可能导致保守探索与激进探索之间的切换失效，从而破坏安全性保障。因此，需要开发一种能够处理延迟并严格约束风险的算法。

Method: 提出名为“Prudent-Banker”的算法，该算法结合了延迟自适应的在线镜像下降（Online Mirror Descent）和改进的分阶段激进探索（phased-aggression）机制。其核心技术贡献是引入了“延迟校准重启阈值”（delay-calibrated restart threshold），用于量化未观测反馈带来的最坏情况偏差并有效识别比较器次优性。

Result: 研究证明了该算法在延迟反馈下能实现 $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+\sqrt{D})$ 的伪后悔值，同时保持对安全比较器的 $\widetilde{O}(1)$ 后悔值。理论下界分析表明，该结果在对数因子内是不可改进的。实验结果验证了该算法在不同延迟分布下均能有效兼顾安全性与学习性能。

Conclusion: Prudent-Banker 算法通过引入延迟校准的重启阈值，成功在对抗性多臂老虎机问题中实现了最优的安全性与稳健性权衡，填补了延迟反馈下安全约束学习的研究空白。该研究不仅提出了最优算法，还推导了相应的理论下界，证明了其在安全基准要求下的后悔值界限已达到最优水平。

Abstract: We study adversarial multi-armed bandits with and without delayed feedback under a safety-aware goal: achieving minimax-optimal worst-case regret while keeping nearly constant regret relative to a designated "safe" baseline policy. Existing approaches can balance this trade-off with immediate feedback for smooth comparators, but arbitrary delays can mistime transitions between conservatism and exploration, endangering the safety guarantee. To bridge this gap, we propose Prudent-Banker, a novel algorithm that combines a delay-adapted variant of Online Mirror Descent with a modified phased-aggression mechanism. Its key technical contribution is a delay-calibrated restart threshold that rigorously accounts for the worst-case distortion induced by unobserved feedback and reliably detects comparator suboptimality. We also establish new lower bounds for safety-constrained adversarial delayed bandits, showing that the regret guarantees of Prudent-Banker are unimprovable, up to logarithmic factors, under the baseline-safety requirement. To the best of our knowledge, Prudent-Banker is the first algorithm to achieve the optimal safety--robustness trade-off: pseudo-regret $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+\sqrt{D})$ together with $\widetilde{O}(1)$ regret against the safe comparator, both with and without delays. Experiments across diverse delay distributions show that, unlike standard delay-robust baselines, Prudent-Banker effectively balances safety and learning.

### [104] [CoSPlay: Cooperative Self-Play at Test-Time with Self-Generated Code and Unit Test](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23491)
*Zhangyi Hu,Chenhui Liu,Tian Huang,Jindong Li,Yang Yang,Jiemin Wu,Zining Zhong,Menglin Yang,Yutao Yue*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前利用可验证奖励（RLVR）和测试时扩展（TTS）的代码生成方法高度依赖代价高昂的真实测试用例（GT UT），且现有的无 GT 测试方法存在自生成测试用例噪声大、与错误代码存在虚假耦合等问题，缺乏一种能够同时优化代码与测试质量的有效机制。

Method: 提出了一种无需训练的协作自博弈框架 CoSPlay：1. 通过探索代码解法识别潜在失败模式，生成具有区分性的测试用例；2. 利用代码-测试用例执行矩阵产生的双向通过率信号，实现代码与测试用例的迭代修剪与优化（协同进化）；3. 当多个代码通过率相同时，通过输出一致性聚类选择最终代码。

Result: 在四个挑战性基准测试上，基于 Qwen2.5-7B 的 CoSPlay 将平均 BoN 从 22.1% 提升至 33.2%，UT 准确率从 14.6% 提升至 78.3%，性能持平或超越了需要训练的 CURE-7B 模型。此外，该方法具有良好的通用性，且随着 token 计算预算的增加，性能持续提升。

Conclusion: CoSPlay 证明了在无需真实测试用例（GT UT）和模型训练的情况下，通过代码与测试用例的协作进化，能够有效提升大型语言模型的代码生成能力。这种方法提供了一种可扩展的推理策略，能够显著改善代码质量并超越现有基准。

Abstract: Recently, Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) and Test-Time Scaling (TTS) have advanced LLM code generation through executable verification. Yet Ground-Truth Unit Tests (GT UTs) remain a bottleneck: SOTA RLVR methods require them for costly training, while existing TTS methods lose competitiveness without them. This motivates GT-free TTS, where existing methods directly use self-generated UTs to refine and select code candidates. Yet such UTs are often noisy or spuriously coupled with wrong code, and UT quality in turn cannot be validated without reliable code. The key challenge is therefore to jointly improve both. To this end, we present CoSPlay, a GT-free, training-free framework that jointly improves codes and UTs through cooperative self-play. It first explores diverse solution ideas and identifies their potential failure modes to produce discriminative UT ideas. It then uses bidirectional pass-count signals from the Code-UT execution matrix to iteratively prune or fix weak codes and refresh or replace unreliable UTs, letting the two pools co-evolve. Finally, when multiple codes remain tied at the highest pass count, it picks the final code from the largest output-consensus cluster, since correct codes agree on the same inputs while wrong codes diverge. Experiments on four challenging benchmarks show that CoSPlay on Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct improves average BoN from 22.1% to 33.2% and UT accuracy from 14.6% to 78.3%, matching or surpassing the RLVR model CURE-7B. When applied to CURE-7B, it further improves BoN by 5.7%. CoSPlay also generalizes across diverse backbones and outperforms GT-free TTS baselines under comparable token budgets, with continued gains as the budget scales up. These results suggest a scalable inference strategy for competitive code generation without any GT data.

</details>


### [105] [Instance-Optimal Estimation with Multiple LLM Judges on a Budget](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23362)
*Junghyun Lee,Sanghwa Kim,Yassir Jedra,Alexandre Proutière,Se-Young Yun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在有限预算下优化LLM评估成本与精度的策略，通过自适应算法实现异构裁判任务分配，在理论与实验层面均验证了其在评分估计中的最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型评估主要依赖“大模型作为裁判（LLM-as-a-judge）”模式，但不同裁判的成本与可靠性各异，且评估任务难度不一。研究旨在解决如何在有限预算下，通过科学分配查询任务以获得最高精度的模型评分估计。

Method: 1. 形式化建模：将问题定义为“预算约束下的异质多裁判估计”；2. 理论分析：推导出最小化误差率的预言机（Oracle）分配方案；3. 算法设计：提出EST-IVWE自适应算法，利用乐观偏差（optimistically biased）方差估计进行资源分配；4. 理论证明：通过Assouad型期望论证推导了局部极小极大下界，证明了算法的实例最优性。

Result: 实验结果表明，相比于传统的均匀分配策略，EST-IVWE算法在合成数据及HelpSteer2数据集上均表现出显著的性能优势，且其理论收敛速度与最优预言机分配方案在渐近意义上一致。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在异构评估环境下，通过自适应的资源分配策略（EST-IVWE），可以在有限预算内达到理论最优的评分估计精度，为大规模语言模型的自动化评估提供了严谨的统计学方法论。

Abstract: Evaluating large language models increasingly relies on LLM-as-a-judge protocols, but such evaluations remain costly: different judges have different prices and reliabilities, and the difficulty of each prompt-response pair can vary substantially. This raises a basic allocation question: under a fixed budget, how should one distribute evaluation queries across heterogeneous judges and instances to obtain the most accurate score estimates? We formalize this question as *budgeted heteroskedastic multi-judge estimation*. Given $K$ prompt-response pairs, $J$ judges with known costs, and unknown query-judge variances, the goal is to estimate a bounded score vector while minimizing an $\ell_p$-error. Our first contribution is to analyze the inverse-variance weighted estimator (IVWE) and to derive the oracle allocation that minimizes its error rate. Since this allocation depends on the unknown variances, we then address the practical unknown-variance setting by proposing EST-IVWE, an adaptive algorithm that constructs and leverages *optimistically biased* variance estimates to stabilize the empirical allocation. We prove that EST-IVWE matches the oracle IVWE rate up to lower-order terms in the budget. Our second and central theoretical contribution is a matching *local* minimax lower bound, which establishes the instance-optimality of the proposed algorithms. A key technical insight is that Fano-type high-probability arguments are too coarse for this problem: their packing construction loses the local variance structure that governs the optimal allocation. We instead use an Assouad-type in-expectation argument, based on local perturbations, which preserves this structure and yields the sharp allocation-dependent lower bound. Finally, we numerically validate the superiority of our approach over naïve uniform allocation on synthetic and HelpSteer2 datasets.

</details>


### [106] [DiLaDiff: Distilled Latent-Augmented Diffusion for Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23605)
*Jean-Marie Lemercier,Tomas Geffner,Karsten Kreis,Morteza Mardani,Arash Vahdat,Ante Jukić*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DiLaDiff通过在连续潜空间中进行扩散采样并结合一致性蒸馏，解决了扩散语言模型生成质量与推理效率的冲突，实现了更快速、高质量的文本生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散语言模型在解码token时难以捕捉token间的内在相关性，导致生成质量与计算效率（吞吐量）之间存在严峻的权衡（trade-off）。

Method: 提出了名为DiLaDiff的三阶段框架：(1) 使用微调后的自动编码器构建具有语义能力的连续潜空间；(2) 训练一个潜扩散模型以学习该潜空间上的先验分布；(3) 引入一致性模型（Consistency Model）对潜扩散模型进行蒸馏，实现快速的多步采样。

Result: 实验表明，DiLaDiff不仅在性能上超越了传统的掩码扩散基准模型，而且显著提升了推理速度。经过一致性蒸馏后，计算开销大幅降低，使得潜空间的生成时间几乎可忽略不计。

Conclusion: DiLaDiff通过将扩散过程从离散的token空间转移到连续的潜空间，并结合一致性模型，成功解决了扩散语言模型在生成质量与推理速度之间的权衡难题，为高效高质量的文本生成提供了新的研究路径。

Abstract: Diffusion language models intrinsically fail to capture correlations between decoded tokens, which leads to a harsh trade-off between sampling quality and throughput. To solve this issue, we propose DiLaDiff, a variant of masked diffusion language models with three components: (1) a continuous latent space with semantic capabilities, learned by an auto-encoder fine-tuned from an existing masked diffusion language model; (2) a latent diffusion model learning the prior over the encoder distribution; (3) a consistency model distilling the learned prior into a few-step latent generative model. We show that, even without distillation, our latent-guided diffusion model outperforms the masked diffusion baseline while significantly accelerating inference. Consistency distillation further lowers the computational overhead of continuous diffusion, such that the latent is generated in negligible time compared to discrete decoding.

### [107] [Score-Based One-step MeanFlow Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23365)
*Kyungyoon Kim,Donghyeon Ki,Hee-Jun Ahn,Byung-Jun Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SOM算法通过将Q函数与得分估计结合，实现了在线强化学习中的高效单步动作生成，解决了传统扩散模型策略推理开销过大的问题，在性能与效率上取得了最佳平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型和流匹配模型虽然在强化学习中表现出色，但其推理时的多步去噪过程带来了巨大的计算开销，难以应用于需要实时决策的在线强化学习场景。而现有的MeanFlow方法在构建目标速度场时依赖于目标分布样本，这在在线RL中是无法获取的。因此，研究旨在解决在线强化学习中高效策略生成的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为SOM（Score-Based One-step MeanFlow Policy Optimization）的演员-评论家（Actor-Critic）算法。该方法利用得分估计（Score Estimation）和概率流常微分方程（Probability Flow ODE），直接从Q函数构建目标速度场，从而将概率质量集中在具有高价值的动作模式上，实现了单步生成策略。

Result: SOM在多个运动控制基准测试中达到了最先进的性能水平。与现有的扩散模型和流匹配策略相比，SOM不仅保持了高性能，还大幅缩短了训练时间和推理时间。

Conclusion: SOM提出了一种创新的在线强化学习策略优化框架，通过单步动作采样实现了与扩散模型相当的性能，同时在计算效率上具有显著优势，为高维连续控制任务提供了高效的决策方案。

Abstract: Diffusion and flow matching have emerged as expressive policy classes in reinforcement learning, but their reliance on multi-step denoising imposes substantial computational overhead at inference time, which is particularly problematic in online RL. MeanFlow offers a promising alternative by learning an average velocity field that maps noise to data in a single network evaluation. However, MeanFlow typically requires samples from the target distribution to construct its target velocity field, which are unavailable in online RL. We propose Score-Based One-step MeanFlow Policy Optimization (SOM), an actor-critic algorithm that resolves this by constructing the target velocity field directly from the Q-function via score estimation and a probability flow ODE, thereby concentrating probability mass on high-value modes. In the fully online RL setting, SOM achieves state-of-the-art performance on locomotion tasks with a single generation step, while substantially reducing both training and inference time compared to prior diffusion- and flow-matching-based policies.

### [108] [Strong Teacher Not Needed? On Distillation in LLM Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23857)
*Taiming Lu,Zhuang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究发现，在大语言模型预训练中，并不一定要盲目追求“强教师模型”。研究表明，弱教师模型同样能有效提升学生模型，且蒸馏效果与教师规模并非简单的正相关，合理的损失混合策略及对过拟合的控制比单纯追求教师的强度更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识蒸馏通常默认“强教师优于弱教师”的范式。本文旨在探究在大语言模型预训练阶段，这一假设是否仍然成立，并试图揭示教师模型能力、训练规模与蒸馏效率之间的真实内在规律。

Method: 研究者通过在大语言模型预训练阶段，系统地改变教师模型与学生模型的架构规模（参数量）以及训练Token预算，构建了强对弱、同等规模、以及弱对强的多种蒸馏关系组合，并对比分析了在不同配置下混合语言建模损失（LM Loss）与知识蒸馏损失（KD Loss）的训练效果，评估了其在域内及域外性能的提升情况。

Result: 1. 即使是规模较小或训练不足的弱教师模型，通过合理的损失函数混合策略，也能有效提升较大规模学生模型的效果；2. 蒸馏收益并非随教师模型能力的增强而无限增长，存在饱和甚至性能反转的现象；3. 知识蒸馏对模型泛化能力（域外数据及下游任务）的提升作用较域内拟合能力更为显著。

Conclusion: 本文挑战了“知识蒸馏必须依赖强教师模型”这一传统观念。研究表明，蒸馏的效果并非线性依赖于教师模型的强弱，合适的蒸馏配置（如损失函数混合）允许弱教师模型辅助强学生模型，且过强的教师模型可能会导致收益饱和甚至下降。研究结果为大语言模型的高效预训练提供了新的策略视角。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation generally assumes a strong-to-weak relationship where stronger teachers yield better students. In this work, we examine this assumption about distillation in large language model pretraining. By varying architecture sizes and training token budgets, we create strong-to-weak, same-level, and weak-to-strong teacher-student relationships, and study distillation's effectiveness under each. We find that the teacher need not be strong: with proper mixing of the language modeling and knowledge distillation losses, even small and undertrained teachers improve larger students. At the same time, a stronger teacher is not always better: pushing the teacher further, through more parameters or more training tokens, can saturate or even reverse the distillation gains. We further observe that distillation improves generalization (out-of-distribution and downstream performance) more readily than in-domain fitting. Together, these results challenge the common belief that distillation pretraining always requires a strong teacher.

### [109] [Every Component is a Lookup: Token Attribution and Composition from a Single Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23393)
*Po-Kai Chen,Niki van Stein,Aske Plaat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 作者提出了一种名为 Unpack 的递归方法，能够仅通过单次前向传播，无需干预或梯度，即可解构 Transformer 模型内部的计算路径与各组件的归因贡献，并在多尺度模型中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Transformer 机制可解释性研究往往难以精确识别模型组件如何组合成计算路径。为了深入理解模型如何通过各子层完成预测，作者旨在开发一种无需复杂外部干预即可揭示内部交互和组件贡献的解构方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Unpack 的递归分解算法。该方法基于 Attention 和 MLP 共享的 φ(S)U 键值模版，通过后向递归将贡献度分解到各子层，计算组件间的交互强度（端到端路径），并实现无需干预、梯度或辅助训练的单次前向传播属性分配。

Result: 在 GPT-2 Small 上成功复现了已知的所有关键计算路径及模式，并能有效区分不同位置相同 token 的贡献度差异（如对重复信息的抑制）。在 Pythia 系列模型（160M 至 6.9B 参数）中，该方法展现了跨尺度的稳健性，能够始终如一地追踪到模型的机制结构。

Conclusion: Unpack 方法证明了通过利用 Transformer 子层的键值（KV）模版结构，无需干预或梯度即可从单次前向传播中有效提取模型内部的计算路径和属性贡献。该研究表明，即便在不依赖预设电路标注的情况下，也能跨模型规模一致地追踪模型的机制结构。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability of transformers requires identifying not just which components matter but how they compose into the computational route that produced a prediction. Both attention and MLP follow a shared key-value template $φ(S)U$. We exploit this structure to develop Unpack, a backward recursion that decomposes credit through both sublayers, producing interaction strengths between any two components, named end-to-end paths with K/Q/V composition labels, and per-token attribution from a single forward pass, without intervention, gradients, or auxiliary training. We evaluate on the indirect object identification task. On GPT-2 small, the method recovers all three composition connections described by Wang et al. (2023), including the mode-specific routing of each connection (K, Q, or V). To test token-level attribution beyond trivial copying, we compare two occurrences of the same name in the same decomposition: the first mention retains strong credit while the duplicate-detection position is suppressed, a pattern absent in matched control prompts. Across the Pythia family from 160M to 6.9B parameters, this suppression pattern is consistently recovered at every scale, demonstrating that the method tracks mechanistic structure without ground-truth circuit labels. Code is available at https://github.com/Fun-Cry/unpacklm.

### [110] [Parametric Prior Mapping Framework for Non-stationary Probabilistic Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23402)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的参数化方法缺乏灵活性，而深度生成模型在处理非平稳时间序列时往往需要大量数据且难以捕获复杂的时序依赖。因此，研究旨在平衡模型的表达能力与鲁棒性，以更有效地建模非平稳多元时间序列。

Method: 提出“参数先验映射”（Parametric Prior Mapping, PPM）框架。该方法通过一个参数化估计器导出一个动态、自适应的先验分布，并利用一个可学习的映射将其注入到生成式建模过程中，从而指导复杂预测分布的学习，并采用混合目标函数进行训练。

Conclusion: PPM框架成功结合了参数化模型的高效性和生成式模型的强表达能力，为非平稳多元时间序列预测提供了一种鲁棒且准确的解决方案，特别是在处理数据非平稳性和不确定性量化方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: Effectively modeling non-stationary dynamics in probabilistic multivariate time series(MTS) forecasting requires balancing expressiveness with robustness. Existing parametric approaches benefit from strong inductive biases but lack flexibility, whereas deep generative models struggle to capture complex temporal dependencies without extensive data and computation. We introduce Parametric Prior Mapping (PPM), a framework that injects parametric structural priors into a generative modeling process. Specifically, PPM utilizes a parametric estimator to derive a dynamic, adaptive prior that guides the learning of a complex predictive distribution via a learnable mapping. This design allows the model to retain the efficiency of parametric methods while exploiting the expressive power of generative models. Trained with a hybrid objective, PPM yields precise forecasts with well-calibrated uncertainty estimates. Empirical results show that PPM outperforms existing baselines in handling non-stationary data, offering a superior trade-off between accuracy and computational efficiency. The code is available at https://github.com/ljl8336/PPM.

### [111] [Hybrid Quantum-Classical Corrective Diffusion Modeling for Meteorological Downscaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23403)
*Rui Wang,Edoardo Pasetto,Amer Delilbasic,Morris Riedel,Kristel Michielsen,Gabriele Cavallaro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将变分量子电路嵌入扩散模型瓶颈层的混合降尺度方案，实验表明该方法在保持天气场物理特征的同时，能有效提升预测精度，但仍面临量子硬件规模限制和跨时间分布泛化性挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 统计降尺度是天气建模的关键，但动力学细化计算成本高昂。研究旨在探索量子计算在处理天气场概率统计降尺度任务中的潜力，验证量子电路是否能作为更高效的非线性特征提取工具。

Method: 提出了一种混合量子-经典纠偏扩散模型。在扩散模型的UNet瓶颈层中嵌入变分量子电路（VQC）层，利用量子电路作为紧凑的非线性特征映射进行潜在空间通道混合，同时保持回归分支为纯经典计算。

Result: 在2020年验证集上，混合量子模型在MAE和CRPS指标上均优于纯经典纠偏扩散模型，且能保持良好的大尺度空间组织性、动能谱及风速分布。但在2021年分布外（OOD）测试中，性能提升未完全保持，显示出一定的泛化能力差距。目前受限于量子硬件的量子比特数量和保真度。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在扩散模型瓶颈层引入量子线路作为非线性特征映射具有可行性，能有效提升降尺度任务的预测精度。然而，量子硬件的规模限制、噪声以及跨分布泛化能力不足是当前应用面临的主要瓶颈。

Abstract: Statistical downscaling is a crucial component of the weather modeling field, where high-resolution outputs must be reconstructed from coarse-resolution inputs with the full cost of dynamical refinement. In this work, we investigate a hybrid quantum-classical corrective diffusion model for probabilistic statistical downscaling of weather fields. The proposed model inserts variational quantum circuit layers into the most compressed bottleneck of the diffusion UNet while leaving the regression branch fully classical. This placement tests whether quantum circuits can act as compact nonlinear feature maps for latent-channel mixing. We evaluate intra-channel and cross-channel ansätze on 10m wind components. On the 2020 validation set, the hybrid models remain stable, preserve the large-scale spatial organization of the generated wind fields, and improve both MAE and CRPS relative to a classical corrective diffusion model in several configurations. Structural diagnostics further show that the hybrid variants preserve kinetic-energy spectra and windspeed distributions similar to its classical counterpart while producing controlled changes in tail behavior, extreme-windspeed localization, and joint wind field components structure. Backend studies on the 2020 validation set show negligible impact from simulated device noise at the tested circuit scale, whereas real-hardware deployment remains limited by qubit availability and execution fidelity. The 2021 out-of-distribution test shows that these in-distribution gains do not transfer uniformly under temporal shift, revealing a generalization gap that motivates future mitigation through stabilization and regularization. These results show that bottleneck-level quantum hybridization can make a nontrivial contribution to weather statistical downscaling, while also highlighting that circuit scale and hardware deployment remain key limiting factors.

### [113] [Sample-wise Targeted Adversarial Attacks on Test-time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23411)
*Phuc Duc Nguyen,Quang Duc Nguyen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种基于元学习（meta-learning）的样本级攻击方法，核心在于一种“优先级感知梯度对齐”（priority-aware gradient alignment）策略。该策略将梯度更新建模为椭圆信任域（ellipsoidal trust-region）问题，在追求攻击成功率的同时，确保模型预测的标签分布与良性基准保持一致，从而实现隐蔽性。

Abstract: Test-time adaptation (TTA) effectively counters distribution shifts but exposes models to adversarial manipulation via the unlabeled test stream. Existing class-wise targeted attacks remain impractical for stealthy exploitation in this setting: since TTA operates on batches, forcing a subset of samples toward a target label unintentionally pulls similar benign samples along, resulting in a conspicuously high frequency of the target label that is easy to detect. To capture a more realistic threat, we introduce a sample-wise targeted attack. Unlike prior approaches, the attacker aims to misclassify only inputs carrying an attacker-chosen trigger, while preserving the global label distribution of benign queries to evade detection. To achieve this, we propose a meta-learning-based attack with a novel priority-aware gradient alignment strategy that explicitly prioritizes attack success. The strategy formulates the gradient update as an ellipsoidal trust-region problem, mitigating the misalignment between attack success and distributional stealth, while providing theoretical guarantees for effective optimization of the attack objective in the presence of gradient misalignment. Extensive experiments on CIFAR-10-C, CIFAR-100-C, and ImageNet-C across TTA protocols demonstrate that our method achieves high targeted success rates while maintaining a label distribution that is consistent with the no-attack baseline, making it difficult to detect in unlabeled TTA deployment scenarios. ### [116] [Hinge Regression Trees and HRT-Boost: Newton-Optimized Oblique Learning for Compact Tabular Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23422)
*Hongyi Li,Jun Xu,Hong Yan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 斜决策树的拆分优化存在离散性和非凸性难题，难以学习到高质量的树结构，现有方法在优化效率和理论保证上仍有提升空间。

Method: 提出了 Hinge Regression Tree (HRT) 框架，将斜分裂重新定义为两个线性预测器的非线性最小二乘问题；引入了基于阻尼牛顿法和回溯线搜索的节点优化策略；构建了 HRT-Boost 集成方法，结合了节点级牛顿更新与阶段性函数梯度下降。

Result: 理论证明 HRT 是具有 O(δ²) 近似率的通用逼近器，且 HRT-Boost 在平方损失下具有经验风险降低保证；实验表明 HRT 相比传统单树表现优异，HRT-Boost 在性能上极具竞争力，且生成的模型更加紧凑。

Conclusion: HRT 和 HRT-Boost 提供了一种高效且理论上稳健的斜决策树构建方法。通过将分裂优化转化为非线性最小二乘问题并结合阻尼牛顿法，该框架在保持模型紧凑性的同时，实现了与现有强基准相当甚至更优的预测性能。

Abstract: Learning high-quality oblique decision trees remains a significant challenge due to the discrete and non-convex nature of split optimization. We present the Hinge Regression Tree (HRT) framework, which reframes each oblique split as a nonlinear least-squares problem over two linear predictors whose max/min envelope induces ReLU-like representation capacity. We show that the resulting node-level optimization can be interpreted as a damped Newton method, and we establish the monotonic decrease of the node objective for its backtracking line-search variant. We establish, theoretically, that HRT is a universal approximator with an explicit $O(δ^2)$ approximation rate. Building upon this base learner, we propose HRT-Boost, a mathematically synergistic ensemble extension that couples node-level Newton updates with stage-wise functional gradient descent. We show that this ensemble construction admits a stage-wise empirical risk reduction guarantee under the squared loss. Empirical evaluations on synthetic and real-world benchmarks show that HRT is highly competitive with established single-tree baselines, and HRT-Boost compares favorably with strong ensemble baselines and often yields substantially more compact models. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/Hongyi-Li-sz/HRT-Boost.

### [117] [Onsager-Machlup Posterior Transport for Deep Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23434)
*Jian Xu,Delu Zeng,John Paisley,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为OM-Path的深度高斯过程推理框架，通过后验传输和Onsager-Machlup路径正则化替代传统的变分推理，显著提升了模型在大规模数据集上的预测性能与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度高斯过程（DGP）中对诱导变量进行近似推理是计算瓶颈。现有方法通常依赖于变分推断（拟合显式密度）或MCMC采样，但这些方法存在计算开销大或精度受限的问题，亟需更有效的推理框架。

Method: 将DGP推理重构为“后验传输（posterior transport）”问题；开发了OM-Path方法，利用概率流ODE（probability-flow ODE）应用于Doob桥接的前向SDE，并使用Onsager-Machlup作用作为路径正则化器，避免了显式密度估计或MCMC采样。

Result: 在七个UCI回归基准测试中，OM-Path在大型数据集上（如power和protein）取得了统计学意义上的显著改进，表现优于基线方法DBVI；在小规模数据集上，尽管部分指标略逊于DBVI，但整体证明了其在处理复杂数据时的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的OM-Path方法将深度高斯过程的推理视为后验传输问题，通过Onsager-Machlup作用正则化的确定性采样器，在大型数据集上表现优于现有的变分推理方法，证明了在路径空间目标函数中降低方差比精确密度估计更为关键。

Abstract: Approximate inference over inducing variables is the central computational bottleneck of Deep Gaussian Processes (DGPs). Existing methods either fit an explicit density $q_φ(\bU)$ by an ELBO (DSVI, IPVI, DDVI, DBVI) or sample by MCMC (SGHMC). We instead frame DGP inference as \emph{posterior transport}: learn a deterministic sampler that maps a tractable reference measure to posterior-relevant inducing variables, regularised by a path prior derived from the Doob-bridged reference diffusion. Our realisation, \textbf{OM-Path} (formally FBVI-bridge-Path), uses Song's probability-flow ODE applied to DBVI's Doob-bridged forward SDE; the reference drift is closed-form from the bridge marginal coefficients (no score matching) and the path regulariser is the \textbf{Onsager--Machlup action}. At the finite-$ε$ value used at training, the objective is the negative log unnormalised density of a tempered Doob-bridge path posterior, and Theorem 1 identifies it with the same posterior's small-noise MAP path via the Freidlin--Wentzell LDP. Two strict path-space ELBO variants on the same bridge backbone (FFJORD log-det; OM-regularised CNF) are derived as ablations. Under a matched-seed paired Wilcoxon test against DBVI on seven UCI regression benchmarks, OM-Path delivers statistically significant wins on the two largest datasets (\textit{power}: $p\!=\!0.014$, NLL $\mathbf{0.012}$ matching the DSVI baseline of $0.017$; \textit{protein}: $p\!=\!0.002$, RMSE $\mathbf{0.716}$ vs.\ $0.764$, NLL $\mathbf{1.086}$ vs.\ $1.149$), statistical ties on \textit{yacht} / \textit{qsar}, and concedes \textit{boston} / \textit{energy} / \textit{concrete} to DBVI on small-$N$ noisy data. The strict-ELBO variants do not clear DBVI on any UCI metric: in this regime, reducing the variance of the path objective dominates exact-density tracking.

### [118] [Automated Random Embedding for Practical Bayesian Optimization with Unknown Effective Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23473)
*Hong Qian,Xiang Shu,Xiang Xia,Xuhui Liu,Yangde Fu,Bei Liang,Huibin Wang,Liang Dou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对高维贝叶斯优化中难以预估有效维度的问题，本文提出了DSEBO方法，通过动态增加子空间维度并共享历史查询数据，实现了在高维空间下的高效优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝叶斯优化在高维场景下受到“维度灾难”的限制。尽管随机嵌入技术可以通过将任务映射到低维子空间来解决该问题，但难以预先确定任务的“有效维度”，而传统的固定维度或反复试验的方法效率低下。因此，研究自动且动态确定子空间维度的方法具有重要意义。

Method: 本文提出了动态共享嵌入贝叶斯优化（DSEBO）。该方法采用一种由低到高的动态维度切换策略：从低维子空间开始，若当前空间收敛则切换至更高维空间。DSEBO基于现有解的质量动态确定下一阶段的子空间维度，并将已查询的样本信息迁移至新子空间以实现更好的初始化。

Result: 理论分析表明DSEBO能够更好地平衡逼近误差与优化误差，并给出了相应的遗憾界。在不同规模的测试函数及未知有效维度的真实任务上的实验表明，DSEBO在优化遗憾和计算时间方面均显著优于现有的先进方法。

Conclusion: DSEBO提供了一种处理高维贝叶斯优化中有效维度未知的有效方案。通过动态调整子空间维度并共享查询样本，该方法在理论上具有更好的遗憾界，并在实验中表现出比现有技术更优的优化效率和收敛性能。

Abstract: Bayesian optimization is widely employed for optimizing complex black-box functions but struggles with the curse of dimensionality. Random embedding, as a dimension reduction strategy, simplifies tasks that possess the effective dimension by optimizing within a low-dimensional subspace. However, determining the effective dimension of a task in advance remains a significant challenge, which influences the selection of the subspace dimensionality and the optimization performance. Traditional methods use fixed subspace dimensions provided by experts or rely on trial and error to estimate subspace dimensions with resources consumed. To this end, this paper proposes an automated random embedding for high-dimensional Bayesian optimization with unknown effective dimension, called Dynamic Shared Embedding Bayesian Optimization (DSEBO). DSEBO starts with a low dimension and switches to a higher subspace if the solutions in the current subspace show preliminary convergence. DSEBO dynamically determines the dimension of the next subspace based on the quality of the solutions in different subspaces and shares the queried solutions with the new subspace for a better initialization. Theoretically, we derive a regret bound for DSEBO and demonstrate that DSEBO can better balance approximation and optimization errors. Extensive experiments on functions with dimensionality of varying magnitudes and real-world tasks with unknown effective dimensions reveal that, compared with state-of-the-art methods, alternating optimization across different subspaces results in significant improvements in high-dimensional optimization, both in terms of optimization regret and time.
