### [119] [Commutator-Induced Uncertainty in VAEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23449)
*Tahereh Dehdarirad,Michael Felsberg,Gabriel Eilertsen,Ziliang Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Lie Group VAE框架，通过诊断潜在空间中的非交换性并利用新的变形稳定性约束，使解码器重构行为与数据内在的非交换结构保持一致，从而提升了生成模型的性能与表示能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对称感知VAE（Symmetry-aware VAEs）通常通过强制代数交换性来处理潜在空间，这在面对非交换性数据时会压制原本有意义的结构特征。本文旨在解决这一问题，提出通过显式诊断并利用重构行为来反映非交换性。

Method: 1. 诊断阶段：在无结构约束下训练模型，利用有限Baker-Campbell-Hausdorff偏差衡量代数非交换性，并通过重构顺序交换测试评估解码器的顺序敏感性；2. 建模阶段：引入变形稳定性约束（deformation-stability constraint），并结合数据驱动的校准常数，将解码器的敏感性与潜在空间的代数非交换性进行对齐；3. 架构设计：将离散生成因子与连续几何变换分离，以提高表示的解耦能力。

Result: 在dSprites、3DShapes、3DCars和CelebA等数据集上的实验表明，该方法在重构质量、潜在空间非交换结构的表示以及因子特定的遍历性方面均优于现有的beta-VAE、CLG-VAE和CFASL等基准模型。特别是在CelebA数据集上，该模型展现了更忠实的重构效果和更具意义的顺序相关交互。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Lie Group VAE框架通过将非交换性视为一种需要建模而非抑制的结构特征，成功地在潜在空间中保留了非交换结构。研究表明，通过对齐代数非交换性与解码器的重构行为，能够显著提升生成模型在处理复杂变换时的准确性与一致性。

Abstract: Variational autoencoders (VAEs) often struggle to represent non-commutative structure in learned latent spaces. Symmetry-aware VAEs commonly address this issue by enforcing commutativity through algebraic regularization, which is appropriate for commutative transformation groups but can suppress meaningful non-commutative structure when it is intrinsic to the data. We argue that non-commutativity should instead be explicitly diagnosed and reflected in reconstruction behavior. We introduce a Lie Group VAE framework that combines geometric and algebraic perspectives on uncertainty while separating discrete generative factors from continuous geometric transformations. In a first phase, the model is trained without structural constraints while algebraic non-commutativity is measured through finite Baker-Campbell-Hausdorff deviations and decoder order sensitivity is measured through reconstruction order-swap tests. These diagnostics reveal a scale mismatch between latent non-commutativity and reconstruction behavior under unconstrained training. In a second phase, we introduce a deformation-stability constraint with a data-driven calibration constant that aligns decoder sensitivity with algebraic non-commutativity. We evaluate the framework on dSprites, 3DShapes, 3DCars, and CelebA against generic and symmetry-aware baselines, including beta-VAE, CLG-VAE, and CFASL. Across synthetic benchmarks, the method improves reconstruction quality and yields decoder-level behavior more consistent with latent non-commutative structure. Qualitative analyses show clearer order-dependent latent compositions and more stable reconstructions. On CelebA, the model yields more faithful reconstructions and factor-specific latent traversals than CFASL, while also exhibiting meaningful order-dependent interactions between learned latent directions.

</details>


### [120] [VACE: Learning Geometrically Structured Representations for Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23504)
*Alberto D. Cencillo,Leonardo Concepción,Isaac Triguero,Julián Luengo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多变量时间序列异常检测，VACE 通过确保正常样本在嵌入空间中形成紧凑且方向一致的轨迹，无需负样本即可实现高效、精准的异常识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于对比学习的异常检测方法往往依赖启发式的负样本采样，难以直接控制潜在空间的几何结构，导致正常样本的聚类不够紧凑，且难以有效捕获异常的时间动力学特征。

Method: 提出了一种名为 VACE（速度对齐通道嵌入）的自监督学习方法。该方法训练一个通道感知编码器，通过“速度一致性”目标（velocity-consistency objective）使正常轨迹在潜在空间中保持局部平滑和方向对齐。测试阶段采用马氏距离（Mahalanobis score）评估分布位置偏离，结合速度库分数（velocity-bank directional score）评估动态异常，实现多维度异常检测。

Result: VACE 在 TSB-AD-M 基准测试中达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能水平，且在模型训练资源消耗较少的情况下，显著优于现有的更复杂算法。

Conclusion: VACE 通过利用时间序列的局部平滑性和方向一致性，在无监督异常检测任务中实现了卓越的鲁棒性和性能，证明了在嵌入空间中显式建模几何结构对于捕捉复杂异常的重要性。

Abstract: Anomaly detection in multivariate time series is a critical task across a wide range of real-world applications, where abnormal behaviour is rare, labels are unavailable, and the cost of a miss is high. The central challenge is learning a characterisation of normality precise enough to flag deviations. Representation self-supervised learning, typically through contrastive approaches, addresses this by embedding temporal patches into a latent space where normality occupies a well-defined region, with anomalies detected by geometric deviation. However, contrastive approaches shape this space indirectly through pair-sampling heuristics, providing no explicit control over the geometric structure that distance-based scoring requires. This means how tightly normal representations are grouped, and whether distances are directionally meaningful. We present VACE (Velocity-Aligned Channel Embeddings), a self-supervised anomaly detection method that represents normality as a compact, directionally coherent region in the embedding space. To this end, VACE trains a channel-aware encoder through a velocity-consistency objective, with no negatives and no synthetic anomalies, so that normal trajectories are locally smooth and aligned. At test time, a Mahalanobis positional score and a velocity-bank directional score are combined multiplicatively, flagging points that are simultaneously off-distribution and dynamically atypical. Despite its simplicity, VACE achieves state-of-the-art performance on TSB-AD-M under rigorous evaluation, significantly outperforming more complex methods trained on substantially larger budgets.

Abstract: We conducted a reproducibility-oriented re-evaluation of prior migraine classification studies, correcting for data leakage and metric bias. ### [122] [Precise: SDE-Consistent Stochastic Sampling for RL Post-Training of Flow-Matching Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23522)
*Jade Zou,Tao Huang,Weijie Kong,Junzhe Li,Yue Wu,Qi Tian,Jiangfeng Xiong,Jianwei Zhang,Liefeng Bo,Zhao Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Precise的新型随机采样器，通过优化SDE调度与引入去噪轨迹一致性近似，解决了强化学习中流匹配模型探索与稳定性的矛盾，显著提升了训练速度与模型对齐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者首先分析了流匹配模型中随机探索与去噪稳定性之间的冲突，推导出了一个新的SDE调度策略。针对现有采样器在RL步骤中离散化误差大和收敛性不佳的问题，提出了名为“Precise”的新型随机采样器。该采样器通过一种冻结干净潜在后验均值（clean-latent posterior mean）的新颖近似方法，确保了去噪轨迹的SDE一致性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的Precise采样器通过保持SDE的一致性并平衡探索与稳定性，为强化学习优化扩散与流匹配模型提供了高效、稳定的解决方案。该方法不仅提升了图像对齐得分，还显著降低了训练所需的计算时间。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become an effective way to improve prompt alignment and perceptual quality in diffusion and flow-matching generators. A critical step for applying online RL to flow matching is turning the deterministic sampling trajectory into a stochastic policy, typically by replacing the reverse-time Ordinary Differential Equation (ODE) with a Stochastic Differential Equation (SDE). The stochastic sampler, controlling the exploration behavior and denoising dynamics, is thus part of the policy, and its design can significantly affect the reward optimization performance. We break down the sampler design into two interdependent components: choosing the right amount of stochastic exploration, and discretizing the resulting SDE faithfully at the small step counts used in RL. To address the first component, we analyze the inherent tension between exploration and stability in denoising and derive an SDE schedule that balances the two. Turning to the discretization challenge, we use a toy example to show that existing samplers can deviate from the flow-matching process, either by introducing excessive discretization noise or by relying on heuristic rules that do not guarantee convergence to the data distribution. To address these issues, we propose Precise, a new stochastic sampler that balances effective exploration with stability. Crucially, Precise keeps the denoising trajectory SDE-consistent through a novel approximation that freezes the clean-latent posterior mean, resolving the excess noise issue in standard samplers. Extensive experiments demonstrate that this formulation leads to significantly faster and more stable reward optimization via reinforcement learning, achieving state-of-the-art alignment scores (e.g., PickScore, HPSv2.1) while requiring 13.1-53.2% less wall-clock training time to match the best in-domain performance of prior samplers.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Reinforcement learning agents often exhibit unintended goal-directed behaviour outside their training distribution, but we currently lack a principled understanding of how such agents will generalise to novel environments based on their training history. We address this gap for agents trained sequentially on one or more tasks. We study over 100 sequential training pipelines, evaluating behaviour across over 250 out-of-distribution environments. We find that salient features drive generalisation, and that goals learnt early in training can persist and influence those acquired later. To explain these phenomena, we introduce latent policy gradients, a method that predicts what out-of-distribution behaviour a training pipeline will likely induce. Our method simulates the evolution of low-dimensional latent variables during training according to what would achieve high reward on the training objective with respect to a simple model of how the latent variables map to behaviour. It achieves strong predictive accuracy, generalises to unseen types of training pipeline, and is interpretable. Our findings demonstrate that while out-of-distribution RL agent behaviour is dependent on the whole training pipeline, this dependence has an underlying structure we can capture, laying groundwork for understanding goal generalisation from a developmental perspective.

*Trinh Pham,Viet Huynh,Hongzhi Yin,Quoc Viet Hung Nguyen,Thanh Tam Nguyen*

TL;DR: MetaEvaluator 是一款创新的模型无关评估框架，通过元学习实现对新模型在无标签数据集上的低成本、高准确度评估，解决了传统评估方法依赖标注和重新训练的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着机器学习模型数量的爆炸式增长，现有的模型评估流程依赖于昂贵的人工标注、重复的微调或特定的模型假设，难以在不同模型架构和模态之间有效扩展，导致在无标签数据上验证新模型可靠性的成本过高。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MetaEvaluator 的模型无关（model-agnostic）框架。该方法利用一组参考模型进行元学习（meta-learning），从而获得可迁移的初始化参数，无需对新模型进行重新训练即可直接在无标签数据集上对新模型进行评估。

Result: 大量实验证明，MetaEvaluator 能够以显著降低的成本，对跨架构和模态的新模型产生稳定且准确的性能评估，首次实现了在完全无标签数据集上对模型进行评估。

Conclusion: MetaEvaluator 是一种高效、通用的无标签模型评估框架，它通过元学习消除了对昂贵人工标注或特定模型重新训练的依赖，为大规模模型基准测试提供了一种经济且实用的解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid growth of machine learning has produced an ever-expanding ecosystem of models, making it increasingly challenging to verify the reliability of newly released models on unseen, unlabeled data. Conventional evaluation pipelines depend on expensive annotation, repeated fine-tuning, or narrow assumptions that fail to transfer across model families. We present MetaEvaluator, a cost-effective, model-agnostic framework for rapid, label-free assessment of unseen models spanning diverse architectures and modalities. MetaEvaluator leverages meta-learning over a pool of reference models to obtain a transferable initialization, enabling accurate evaluation of new models while amortizing cost across the pool and removing the need for per-model retraining. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first model-agnostic framework capable of evaluating new models on entirely unlabeled datasets. Extensive experiments show that MetaEvaluator produces stable and accurate performance estimates at substantially reduced cost compared to conventional approaches, making scalable benchmarking of emerging models on unlabeled data practical.

### [125] [Preisach Attention: A Hysteretic Model of Sequential Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23603)
*Piotr Frydrych*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于磁滞算子的新型序列建模架构 PAL，通过利用极值栈替代 Softmax 注意力，在保持高效推理（O(n log n)）的同时，能够更好地捕捉长序列中的历史统计特征，并具备独特的速率独立性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对传统 Transformer 在处理长序列时计算开销大（O(n^2)）以及对位置信息依赖较强的问题，作者试图从数学物理学中的经典 Preisach 磁滞算子中汲取灵感，寻找一种能够高效处理长序列记忆、具备速率独立性且计算更轻量的新型建模架构。

Method: 本文提出了一种新型的 Preisach 注意力层 (PAL)，用基于学习阈值的二值继电器算子取代了传统的 Softmax 注意力机制，并利用极值栈作为内部状态来处理序列数据，实现了对输入序列历史的压缩与跟踪。

Result: PAL 架构在理论上证明了其单层即可实现图灵完备性（优于标准 Transformer 的 O(log n) 层），且在处理历史范围统计等任务上比传统 Transformer 更具优势。此外，PAL 的推理成本降低至 O(n log n)，并表现出良好的速率独立性。

Conclusion: 本文引入的 Preisach 注意力层 (PAL) 为序列建模提供了一种基于经典磁滞算子的非传统架构。它通过利用极值栈捕捉历史动态，实现了比传统 Transformer 更高效的长期依赖建模，且在计算复杂度和理论表达能力上展示了独特的优势与权衡。

Abstract: We introduce the Preisach Attention Layer (PAL), a novel sequence modelling architecture grounded in the classical Preisach hysteresis operator from mathematical physics. PAL replaces the softmax attention mechanism with a binary relay operator parameterised by learned activation and deactivation thresholds, maintaining a stack of local extrema as its internal state. A single-layer PAL-Transformer with O(1) depth is Turing-complete under arbitrary precision arithmetic, achievable through simulation of a two-stack pushdown automaton -- in contrast to the O(log n) depth required by standard hard-attention transformers. Second, we prove that the function classes computable by PAL and by the transformer are incomparable: PAL computes historical range statistics in O(1) layers that require O(log n) layers for transformers, while transformers support random-access retrieval that PAL cannot perform without auxiliary state. The separating property is rate-independence -- PAL responds only to the sequence of local extrema, not to absolute token positions or temporal spacing. Third, we show that the extremum stack constitutes a minimal sufficient statistic of the input history for all rate-independent functionals, providing a formal analogue of the wiping property in classical hysteresis theory. PAL is thus an efficient architecture for tasks with long episodic memory and weak positional dependence, with O(n log n) total inference cost versus O(n^2) for standard attention.

### [126] [Learning Through Noise: Why Subliminal Learning Works and When It Fails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23645)
*Vincent C. Brockers,Roman D. Ventzke,Valentin Neuhaus,Belén Hidalgo-Ogalde,Viola Priesemann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了“潜意识学习”的核心机制在于输出头的兼容性而非初始化参数的一致性，通过实验证明了即使在不同模型架构下，通过兼容的输出头也能实现知识的有效迁移，并提供了预测该现象发生边界的理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既往研究认为“潜意识学习”（在任务无关的数据上进行蒸馏而产生的知识迁移）主要归因于师生模型初始化参数的一致性。本文旨在挑战这一观点，探索是否存在更本质的驱动因素，并试图为潜意识学习建立一个系统性的理论框架，以解释其发生机制并确定其局限性。

Method: 作者构建了一个受控的MNIST实验环境，通过将输出拆分为“辅助头”（用于处理任务无关的噪声信号）和“分类头”（用于正常分类任务）。在此架构下，研究者系统性地测试了随机初始化隐藏层、增删层数以及改变模型架构（如从MLP切换到CNN）等多种情形，以验证输出头兼容性对知识迁移的影响，并据此推导了潜意识学习失效的理论上限。

Result: 实验结果表明，即使模型架构不同、隐藏层随机初始化，只要具备兼容的辅助输出头，学生模型就能成功接收来自教师模型的信号，使自身的表征向教师靠拢。当分类头也保持兼容时，仅在任务无关噪声上训练的学生模型，其性能甚至能接近或达到教师模型的水平。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了“潜意识学习”并非依赖于师生模型初始化参数的高度相似，而是由兼容的输出头（output heads）所驱动。通过将该效应理论化，研究者不仅揭示了其运作机制，还明确了其表现的边界，使该现象从一种意外的迁移效应转变为一种具有预测性的理论机制。

Abstract: In the context of artificial neural networks, subliminal learning refers to the transfer of task-relevant knowledge or unintended biases from teacher to student models through distillation on task-unrelated input$\unicode{x2013}$output pairs. Prior explanations tie this effect to shared or closely matched teacher$\unicode{x2013}$student initialization. We show that a closely matched initialization is not necessary. Instead, subliminal learning is governed by compatible output heads. Using a controlled MNIST setting, we split outputs into an auxiliary head (for auxiliary, task-unrelated noise signals) and a class head (for classification) to demonstrate subliminal learning occurs$\unicode{x2014}$even when we randomly initialize hidden layers and remove layers, add new layers, or change the architecture (MLP-to-CNN). Compatible auxiliary heads enable transfer of a recoverable teacher signal, bringing the student's representations closer to the teacher's. When the class heads remain compatible as well, students trained only on task-unrelated noise can approach, and in favorable regimes match, teacher-level task performance. Our setting enables us to develop a theory that explains the mechanism of subliminal learning and to derive upper bounds on when subliminal learning fails. Together, our results turn subliminal learning from a surprising transfer effect into a theoretically grounded mechanism with predictable limits.

</details>


### [127] [It's the humans, not the data: Geopolitical bias in LLMs originates in post-training, amplified by the language of the prompt](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23825)
*Stuart Bladon,Brinnae Bent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了地缘政治偏见源于预训练数据的传统认知，证明了偏见主要是在后训练阶段被主动塑造的，且往往向模型开发商的母国或母语倾向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 学术界普遍认为大语言模型中的地缘政治偏见源于预训练阶段使用的大规模互联网数据。本研究旨在验证这一假设，探究地缘政治偏见在模型生命周期（预训练阶段与后训练阶段）中的具体起源。

Method: 研究人员选取了来自7家实验室的7对开放权重的大语言模型（包含预训练基础模型和后训练聊天模型），通过配对场景强制选择测试（paired-scenario forced-choice probe），在英语、法语和中文语境下，对28组国家对进行了偏见检测，并对比了基础模型与聊天模型之间的偏见偏移。

Result: 研究发现：1. 地缘政治偏见主要在后训练阶段产生；2. 六家实验室的模型在后训练后，表现出了向模型开发方所属国家或地区倾斜的偏见；3. 这种偏见偏移在特定语言提示下更为显著（如Mistral模型在法语提示下表现出更强的亲法倾向）。以Qwen 2.5为例，其聊天模型相比基础模型出现了显著的亲华偏见偏移。

Conclusion: 研究表明大语言模型的地缘政治偏见并非完全源于预训练数据，而是主要在后训练阶段被主动塑造。这一发现凸显了对模型对齐过程（alignment process）进行更高透明度审查和监督的必要性，以防止模型在代表国家、文化和政治观点时出现偏见。

Abstract: It has generally been assumed that geopolitical bias in language models originates from the training data used during the pre-training phase. We tested seven open-weight LLM pairs consisting of the base model (pre-training only) and the chat model (pre-training and post-training) from seven labs on a paired-scenario forced-choice probe over 28 country pairs in English, French, and Chinese, and found that geopolitical bias originates in post-training rather than in pre-training. Across seven AI labs, six showed shifts in the direction associated with the country or region of the model developer after post-training. This shift is strongest in Alibaba's Qwen 2.5: while the base is neutral on China-favourability (-0.15 log-odds, p=0.15), the post-trained chat variant is at +2.91 (p<10^-4), an 18x shift in odds. We also observe shifts in biases toward other countries across all models. Additionally, the magnitude of this shift depends on the language used to prompt the model: the French-made Mistral becomes pro-France only under French prompting (FR-EN shift +1.91, p<10^-4). These findings suggest that geopolitical preferences in language models are not simply inherited from large-scale internet data but are actively shaped during post-training, highlighting the need for greater transparency, auditing, and oversight of alignment processes that influence how models represent nations, cultures, and political perspectives.

*Aneesh Komanduri,Xintao Wu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的因果生成模型通常需要在训练阶段集成因果约束，缺乏统一的框架来充分利用预训练基础模型强大的零样本推理能力，导致其在处理复杂视觉任务时的灵活性和通用性受限。

Conclusion: FM-CGM 为利用预训练基础模型进行视觉因果推理提供了一个模块化且有效的框架，证明了在无需微调的情况下实现零样本因果发现与反事实生成的可能性，同时也为确保语义一致性和因果传导提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Causal generative modeling is essential for developing reliable and transparent AI systems capable of counterfactual reasoning. While existing approaches focus on integrating causal constraints during the training of generative models, they often lack a unified framework to leverage the zero-shot reasoning capabilities of pretrained foundation models. We introduce FM-CGM, a modular framework for end-to-end visual causal reasoning using pretrained foundation models. FM-CGM formalizes the causal pipeline through three core components: a concept extractor, a concept manipulator, and a counterfactual generator. By leveraging a large reasoning model for causal inference and a text-to-image diffusion model for generation, our approach enables zero-shot causal discovery, intervention, and counterfactual generation. We then develop Causal Semantic Guidance (CSG), a cross-attention-based mechanism that ensures semantic interventions propagate to descendant concepts while preserving invariant regions. We empirically show that our approach can identify plausible causal structures and is suitable for faithful counterfactual image generation.

### [129] [When One Point Is Not Enough: Addressing Ambiguous Instances in Dimensionality Reduction by Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23540)
*Diede P. M. van der Hoorn,Alessio Arleo,Fernando V. Paulovich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对降维分析中“模糊实例”导致的数据点局部结构丢失问题，本文提出了一种通过复制这些实例来还原多重邻域归属的图算法，显著提升了高维数据可视化的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的降维（DR）方法在投影过程中不可避免地会丢失信息，产生视觉伪影。作者特别指出，当一个高维数据点属于多个不相关邻域时（即“模糊实例”），由于标准DR方法将其映射为单一投影点，导致无法完整表示其邻域结构（即“部分邻域嵌入”），从而造成严重的误导。

Method: 提出了一种基于图的方法，能够自动识别高维空间中与多个互不相似的邻域高度相似的“模糊实例”，并允许在低维投影中将这些实例复制为多个点，使每个副本分别置于其对应的邻域中。该方法可与UMAP等基于局部图的降维技术结合使用。

Result: 实验表明，该方法能够揭示降维投影中原本被隐藏的邻域归属关系，有效减少了部分邻域嵌入现象，并通过定量分析验证了其在改善局部结构保真度方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过复制“模糊实例”可以有效缓解降维过程中的部分邻域嵌入问题，从而在低维投影中更忠实地呈现复杂的高维数据局部结构，并增强了可视化分析的准确性。

Abstract: Dimensionality Reduction (DR) methods are widely used to visualize high-dimensional data. One key task in DR-based analysis is discovering neighborhoods, which relies on analyzing the fine-grained local structure of a projection. However, DR is an inherently lossy process; no technique can perfectly preserve the high-dimensional relationships, and projections therefore contain visual artifacts. In this paper, we highlight a typically overlooked source of visual artifacts: ambiguous instances. These are instances that are highly similar to multiple mutually dissimilar neighborhoods in the high-dimensional space. Standard DR methods cannot faithfully project such instances, since each data instance is mapped to a single point in the visual space. As a result, such an instance is placed in only one of its neighborhoods (or in none at all), so only part of its neighborhood structure is represented. We call this distortion partial neighborhood embedding. In this paper, we introduce a graph-based approach that identifies ambiguous instances and replicates them as multiple points in the projection, placing each copy within its respective neighborhood. We use UMAP for our results, but our approach also generalizes to other local graph-based DR techniques, and we show that our approach reveals previously hidden neighborhood memberships in projections and reduces partial neighborhood embedding across multiple examples, and is further supported by quantitative analyses.

### [130] [LLMs as Noisy Channels: A Shannon Perspective on Model Capacity and Scaling Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23901)
*Xu Ouyang,Deyi Liu,Yuhang Cai,Jing Liu,Yuan Yang,Chen Zheng,Thomas Hartvigsen,Yiyuan Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于香农-哈特利定理的“香农缩放定律”，将LLM训练建模为有噪信道通信，成功解释并预测了在大规模训练中出现的非单调性能衰退现象，弥补了现有幂律模型的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM缩放定律（Scaling Laws）大多基于单调幂律，无法解释在大规模计算资源增加时出现的“灾难性过拟合”或量化诱导的性能退化等非单调现象。研究旨在建立一个更通用的统一框架，以解释并预测性能从单调上升到U型衰减的转变。

Method: 该研究提出了“香农缩放定律”，将LLM训练过程类比为有噪信道上的信息传输。通过引用香农-哈特利定理，将模型参数映射为信道带宽，将训练Token映射为信号功率。通过量化学习信号与内在噪声之间的相互作用，构建了一个能够捕捉非单调性能变化的数学框架。

Result: 实验在Pythia和OLMo2模型上进行了验证，结果表明：1. 香农缩放定律在预测性能波动方面优于传统缩放定律；2. 该定律准确预测了丢失的“损失盆地”（loss basins）；3. 在外推实验中，该定律展现了极强的泛化能力，能够准确预测未见过的更大规模模型（如12B参数模型）的性能表现。

Conclusion: 香农缩放定律证明了LLM的性能存在“香农容量”限制，超越该限制会因为信噪比（SNR）不足而导致性能下降。通过这一框架，该研究不仅统一了模型性能的缩放预测，还揭示了模型训练中从单调改进到U型退化的本质机制。

Abstract: Existing scaling laws for Large Language Models (LLMs), predominantly monotonic power laws, fail to explain emerging non-monotonic phenomena such as catastrophic overtraining and quantization-induced degradation, where performance deteriorates despite increased compute.
  We propose the Shannon Scaling Law, a unified theoretical framework that models LLM training as information transmission over a noisy channel, grounded in the Shannon-Hartley theorem. By mapping model parameters to channel bandwidth and training tokens to signal power, our formulation explicitly captures the interaction between learning signal and intrinsic noise. This perspective reveals a fundamental Shannon capacity for LLMs: scaling model size or data without preserving a sufficient signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) inevitably amplifies noise, inducing a transition from monotonic improvement to U-shaped performance degradation.
  We validate our theory through experiments on Pythia and OLMo2 under perturbations, including Gaussian noise, quantization and supervised fine-tuning on math, QA and code tasks. The Shannon Scaling Law consistently outperforms classical scaling laws and recent perturbation-aware laws, achieving strong $R^2$ scores and accurately capturing loss basins missed by prior approaches. It also extrapolates: fitted on $\leq$6.9B Pythia models with $\leq$180B tokens, it predicts the unseen 12B model up to 307B tokens at pooled $R^2{=}0.847$, while monotonic baselines collapse.

</details>


### [131] [Is Dimensionality a Barrier for Retrieval Models?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23556)
*Kiril Bangachev,Guy Bresler,Jonathan Kogan,Yury Polyanskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从理论上解释了低维嵌入为何能支持超大规模检索，证明了维度 $O(k\log (n/k))$ 对实现最优间隔的必要性与充分性，并指出 Sigmoid 损失比 InfoNCE 更能有效提升嵌入质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究为何典型的低维度嵌入（$d \approx 1000$）能够支持数十亿甚至数万亿规模的数据点检索，试图从理论上解释嵌入维度、数据规模与表示质量（通过最大间隔来衡量）之间的缩放关系。

Method: 本文采用理论分析与经验验证相结合的方法。理论上，通过分析最大间隔嵌入（Maximal-margin embeddings）的通信复杂性，给出了嵌入维度与间隔之间的界限，并证明了该界限的紧凑性；实验上，通过对比实验评估了 InfoNCE 和 Sigmoid 损失函数在构建大间隔嵌入时的效果。

Result: 建立了维度与最大间隔之间的理论边界，指出当 $d = O(k\log (n/k))$ 时，可以达到最优的表示间隔 $\Theta(k^{-1/2})$；证明了该界限在特定设置下的最优性，并提供了在受限维度下的构造方法，同时实证了 Sigmoid 损失在优化表示质量方面的优势。

Conclusion: 本文证明了在嵌入检索模型中，维度 $d = O(k\log (n/k))$ 对于实现最大化间隔是必要且充分的，并明确了该结论下维度的缩放定律。此外，实验表明 Sigmoid 损失函数在产生大间隔嵌入方面优于 InfoNCE 损失。

Abstract: Why does the low dimensionality of representations, typically $d\approx 1000$, not prevent modern embedding-based retrieval models from scaling to billions, or even trillions, of data points? To answer this question, we study maximal-margin embeddings in the following retrieval model, classically studied in communication complexity [PS86] and more recently in embedding-based retrieval [WBNL26]. Let $A\in \{0,1\}^{N\times n}$ be a matrix indicating whether each of $N$ queries is relevant to each of $n$ documents. We are interested in the largest margin $m>0,$ denoted by $\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(d, A),$ for which there exist unit norm embeddings of the queries and documents $\{U_j\}_{j = 1}^N, \{V_i\}_{i = 1}^n$ with the following property. $\langle U_j, V_i\rangle \ge m$ whenever $A_{ji} = 1$ and $\langle U_j, V_i\rangle \le -m$ otherwise. A large margin is a key proxy for representation quality: it controls both robustness to perturbations and compositional generalization across queries. Our main theorem establishes that the best possible margin without a restriction on the dimension, $\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(+\infty, A),$ can be nearly achieved in dimension $d = O(\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(+\infty, A)^{-2}\log n)$ which improves a theorem of [BDES02]. Together with a matching lower bound in Theorem 1.5, we conclude that when $A\in \{0,1\}^{\binom{n}{k}\times n}$ is the matrix containing all possible $k$-sparse rows once, dimension $d = O(k\log (n/k))$ is necessary and sufficient for the maximal possible margin $\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(+\infty, A) = Θ(k^{-1/2})$ in this setting. This fully resolves the setup of [WBNL26]. We also give several constructions for large margins when $d = o(k\log (n/k)).$ Finally, we empirically test the InfoNCE and sigmoid losses for producing large margin embeddings and demonstrate a clear advantage of the sigmoid loss.

</details>


### [132] [MARS: Magnitude-Aware Rank Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23563)
*Muhammad Rajabinasab,Afsaneh M. Nejad,Arthur Zimek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对机器学习评估中 CD 图存在的“量级盲区”问题，提出了一种名为 MARS 的改进方法，通过引入相对性能差距作为权重来优化秩统计，从而提供更准确的性能比较结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习模型评估方法中，关键差异（CD）图普遍依赖离散的秩（rank），这种做法忽略了模型间性能差距的真实幅度，导致所谓的“量级盲区”问题，难以准确反映模型性能的微小或巨大差异。

Method: 提出了一种名为“幅度感知秩统计（MARS）”的方法。该方法引入了一个“相对边际系数”作为离散秩的权重，该系数根据模型在数据集上的最佳与最差表现之间的距离对秩进行缩放，并通过动态投影处理边界情况，从而改进了传统的关键差异（CD）图计算过程。

Result: 实验结果表明，MARS 能够产生更具现实意义的统计表现，在广泛的实验设置中提供了比标准 CD 图更深刻的性能对比见解，有效克服了传统方法对性能幅度不敏感的缺陷。

Conclusion: MARS 弥补了传统 CD 图的“量级盲区”，提供了一种更符合机器学习模型真实性能差异的评估手段，不仅使统计结果更加客观，还为研究者提供了更具深度的方法表现洞察。

Abstract: Comprehensive evaluation of machine learning models is the key to make sure that they perform as robustly and consistently as desired. In order to summarize the experimental results and pick a winner, Critical Difference (CD) diagrams are used. Standard CD diagrams rely on discrete ranks, discarding the magnitude of performance gaps between models, raising an issue which we call magnitude-blindness. In order to address this issue, we propose Magnitude-Aware Rank Statistics (MARS) that incorporates a relative margin coefficient as a weight for the discrete ranks. This coefficient scales ranks based on the distance between the best and worst performers, with a dynamic projection to handle boundary cases. Followed by the calculation of a CD value, MARS results in a more realistic statistical representation of differences of model performances and more insights on how methods actually perform in vast and extensive experimental settings.

</details>


### [133] [Push Your Agent: Measuring and Enforcing Quantitative Goal Persistence in Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23574)
*Yuandao Cai,Yuzhang Zhu,Liyou Gao,Wensheng Tang,Shengchao Qin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对语言智能体在长周期任务中无法完成定量目标的问题，本文提出了定量目标持久性（QGP）概念及PushBench基准测试，验证了通过状态追踪和工作单元追踪机制，能显著提升智能体在复杂、大规模任务中的可靠性和持续执行能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长周期语言智能体往往能够执行合理的局部工具调用，但常在未完成预定数量的目标前就提前终止工作。研究者希望解决这种“定量目标持久性”缺失的问题，以量化和改善智能体在长周期任务中的可靠性。

Method: 1. 提出了“定量目标持久性”（QGP）的概念，定义了智能体在达到指定数量的验证目标前持续工作的能力。
2. 构建了PushBench基准测试，通过外部验证器强制执行任务，精确衡量重复提交、伪完成和进度漂移等指标。
3. 比较了多种控制器设计，包括状态追踪检索控制器和积压工作单元追踪控制器。
4. 在Claude Code (Sonnet 4.6) 和 Codex CLI等前沿模型上进行了大规模任务性能评估。

Result: 1. 状态追踪检索控制器表现最优，成功率达69-78%，并消除了重复提交。
2. 积压工作单元追踪控制器在标准模型完全失败的条件下，仍能达到25-50%的成功率。
3. 前沿模型（Claude Code, Codex CLI）在处理50个工件的任务时表现尚可，但在规模扩大到100个工件时，任务成功率显著下降，显示出长周期任务的可靠性短板。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了定量目标持久性（QGP）是语言智能体面临的一个关键可靠性挑战。实验表明，仅具备局部工具使用能力不足以完成大规模任务；智能体需要能够进行状态追踪和进度验证，才能在长周期工作中保持持续的输出并最终完成目标。

Abstract: Long-horizon language agents can make many plausible local tool calls yet fail to persist until a requested count is actually complete. We study this gap as Quantitative Goal Persistence (QGP): whether an agent keeps working until an external verifier confirms enough distinct valid items. PushBench turns this into a benchmark for repository-artifact collection and verifier-backed work units, so repeated work, duplicate submissions, false completion, and progress drift are measured directly rather than hidden behind a final success flag. In matched controller comparisons, a state-tracking retrieval controller reaches 69-78% success while eliminating duplicate submissions, and a backlog-tracking work-unit controller reaches 25-50% success in settings where standard and completion-gated controllers complete no task instances. Black-box frontier-agent evaluations with Claude Code (Sonnet 4.6) and Codex CLI (gpt-5.4) solve many 50-artifact tasks but drop to 3 out of 9 successes per condition at 100 artifacts. The results show that quantitative goals stress a different reliability requirement from local task competence: agents must maintain verified progress and stop only when the requested work is complete.

</details>


### [134] [Valid and Expressive Copulas for Irregular Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23632)
*Christian Klötergens,Tom Hanika,Lars Schmidt-Thieme,Vijaya Krishna Yalavarthi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CopFITi 是一种专为不规则多变量时间序列设计的概率预测模型，它通过将归一化流与高斯混合 Copula 相结合，实现了边缘分布与联合依赖结构的有效解耦，提升了建模的准确性与一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多变量时间序列预测模型通常直接拟合联合分布，难以有效处理不规则采样且灵活性不足。研究者旨在通过解耦边缘分布和联合依赖结构，提升模型处理不规则多变量时间序列的表达能力与预测准确性。

Method: 该模型采用了一种混合架构：利用归一化流（Normalizing Flows）对单变量边缘分布进行高表达能力的建模，并结合高斯混合 Copula（Gaussian Mixture Copula）来捕捉复杂的联合依赖结构。该设计通过构造确保了模型在边缘化操作上的一致性。

Result: 实验结果表明，与直接拟合全联合分布的架构相比，基于 Copula 的解耦方法能够构建更优的边缘模型。CopFITi 在不规则多变量时间序列的联合密度建模任务上达到了新的最先进（SOTA）水平。

Conclusion: CopFITi 证明了将边缘分布与联合依赖结构解耦的策略在不规则多变量时间序列（IMTS）预测中具有显著优势。通过构建满足边缘化一致性的 Copula 模型，该方法成功设定了联合密度建模的新基准。

Abstract: We introduce CopFITi, a copula model for probabilistic forecasting of irregular multivariate time series (IMTS). Our model combines the expressivity of normalizing flows for univariate marginals with the consistency and flexibility of a Gaussian Mixture Copula for the joint dependency structure. Our experiments show that copula-based approaches, which decouple the marginals from the joint, yield better marginal models than architectures that directly fit the full joint. With CopFITi, we propose the first IMTS copula that is marginalization-consistent by construction and establish a new state of the art in joint IMTS density modeling.

</details>


### [135] [Optimal Dimension-Free Sampling for Regularized Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23726)
*Meysam Alishahi,Alexander Munteanu,Simon Omlor,Jeff M. Phillips*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套针对多种分类损失函数的最优采样方案，通过高阶矩分析改进了现有算法，实现了接近最优的采样复杂度界限，并提供了严谨的上下界证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的采样界限（如Alishahi和Phillips提出的$k^3/\varepsilon^2$敏感度采样）在复杂度上不够理想。作者旨在为Logistic、Hinge及ReLU等广泛使用的分类损失函数寻找更紧凑、最优的采样界限，并探究正则化项对采样复杂度的具体影响。

Method: 本文摒弃了传统的VC维和敏感度框架（该框架通常导致较差的界限），而是采用了一种结合高阶矩界限和经验过程分析的方法。通过简单的均匀采样或平方范数采样策略，利用Lipschitz连续性，证明了在不同正则化条件下采样复杂度的上下界。

Result: 本文证明了多类损失函数的最优采样界限：对于$\|\cdot\|_2/k$正则化，界限为$k^2/\varepsilon^2$；对于$\|\cdot\|_1/k$正则化，界限为$k/\varepsilon^2$；对于$\|\cdot\|_2^2/k$正则化，在满足特定导数约束条件下可实现线性复杂度，否则为$k^2/\varepsilon^2$。同时证明了当$g(0)=0$时，不存在与维度无关的采样界限。这些上界均有对应的下界支持。

Conclusion: 本文通过精细的矩分析和经验过程论证，确立了针对多种Lipschitz连续分类损失函数的最优采样界限。研究结果不仅在数学上严谨地证明了上下界，还打破了现有基于VC维和敏感度框架的复杂性限制，为在大规模数据集上高效地进行近似学习提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We prove optimal sampling bounds achieving $(1\pm\varepsilon)$-relative error for a broad class of Lipschitz continuous classification loss functions under various regularization terms. This includes important functions such as logistic and sigmoid loss, hinge loss, and ReLU loss, as prominent and popular representative examples. In particular, we prove $k^2/\varepsilon^2$ upper and lower bounds for $\|\cdot\|_2/k$ regularization, and $k/\varepsilon^2$ upper and lower bounds for $\|\cdot\|_1/k$ regularization. For $\|\cdot\|_2^2/k$ regularization, the sampling complexity depends mainly on a bounded derivative property: if $|g'(x)|\leq g(x)$, and $g(0)>0$, and $g$ is monotonic or convex, then it admits linear in $k$ sampling complexity; otherwise the general bound is $k^2/\varepsilon^2$. However, if $g(0)=0$, our results indicate that no dimension-free bounds are possible, and even sublinear bounds are ruled out. All upper bounds are complemented by matching lower bounds up to polylogarithmic terms. Moreover, our work relies conceptually and algorithmically on simple uniform or (squared) norm sampling and hereby improves over recent cubic $k^3/\varepsilon^2$ sensitivity sampling bounds of (Alishahi and Phillips, ICML'24). This is achieved by refined arguments involving higher moment bounds and empirical process analyses to avoid overcounting that appears in the de-facto standard VC-dimension and sensitivity framework.

</details>


### [136] [Approaching I/O-optimality for Approximate Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23751)
*Pál András Papp,Aleksandros Sobczyk,Anastasios Zouzias*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了注意力机制的 I/O 复杂度，提出了一种将复杂度从平方级 $O(n^2)$ 降低至近线性 $O(n)$ 的新算法，并证明了该算法在理论上接近最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型注意力机制的实现（如 FlashAttention）在 I/O 复杂度上依赖于序列长度 $n$ 的平方，这在处理长序列时导致了显著的内存访问瓶颈。作者旨在探索注意力机制计算的本质 I/O 下界，并寻求实现接近该下界的近线性算法。

Method: 研究借鉴了 Alman 和 Song 的近似注意力计算框架，通过设计新的 I/O 高效算法，实现了对输入数据的高效分块与存取。同时，作者通过理论分析，针对不同参数区域推导出了相应的 I/O 下界，以验证算法的逼近最优性。

Result: 研究成功提出了一种在大多数参数条件下，I/O 复杂度仅与 $n$ 近线性相关的注意力计算方法。通过严格的数学证明，作者展示了该方法在理论上接近 I/O 最优，突破了传统方法中平方级复杂度的限制。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，在大多数参数设定下，注意力机制的 I/O 复杂度可以达到近乎线性的 $O(n)$，而非先前认为的平方级。通过开发 I/O 高效算法并提供相应的下界证明，研究证明了现有注意力计算方法存在优化空间，并给出了接近理论最优的解决方案。

Abstract: We revisit the I/O complexity of attention in large language models. Given query-key-value matrices $Q,K,V\in\mathbb{R}^{n\times d}$, and a machine with fast memory size $M$, the goal is to compute the "attention matrix" $A=\text{softmax}(Q K ^{\top}/\sqrt{d}) V$ with the minimal number of data transfers between fast and slow memory. Existing methods in the literature, most notably FlashAttention and its variants, incur an I/O cost that depends quadratically on $n$, while a trivial lower bound only requires $Ω(nd)$ I/O's to read the inputs and write the output. In this work, we present a technique for computing attention where the I/O cost only depends almost-linearly on $n$ in most parameter regimes. This is achieved by developing I/O-efficient algorithms inspired by the recent approximate attention framework of Alman and Song. We also prove corresponding lower bounds in each parameter regime to show that our algorithms are indeed close to I/O-optimal.

</details>


### [137] [LLM-driven design of physics-constrained constitutive models: two agents are better than one](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23754)
*Marius Tacke,Matthias Busch,Kian Abdolazizi,Jonas Eichinger,Kevin Linka,Roland Aydin,Christian Cyron*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多智能体LLM框架，通过“创建-审查”闭环机制，确保自动生成的本构模型严格遵守物理定律，从而实现了高精度、物理有效且可靠的自动化模型构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统本构模型开发门槛高，现有的单智能体LLM生成方法缺乏对模型是否遵循物理定律的系统性检查，导致生成的模型可能存在物理一致性问题，难以直接用于工程实践。

Method: 提出了一种多智能体大语言模型框架：由“创建者（Creator）”智能体负责根据数据生成本构模型，由“审查者（Inspector）”智能体根据九项基本物理约束对模型进行批判性审核，若发现违规则返回修正，直至模型完全符合物理定律。

Result: 在脑组织、实验橡胶和合成橡胶等数据集上的测试表明，引入审查机制后，模型满足物理约束的比例显著提升（Claude Opus达到100%），同时模型保持了高精度，并表现出良好的外推泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过将模型生成与物理审查分离，多智能体架构使基于大语言模型的本构模型构建过程变得更加可信、可靠且具备实际应用价值，为自动化、物理感知模型发现提供了通用且可扩展的新路径。

Abstract: Developing constitutive models that capture how materials deform under load traditionally requires years of specialized expertise in continuum mechanics, machine learning, and scientific programming. Large language models (LLMs) have recently been shown to lower this barrier by generating constitutive models on demand, but existing single-agent pipelines lack systematic checks that the resulting models respect fundamental physical laws. To close this gap, we introduce the first multi-agent LLM-driven approach for constitutive model generation: a Creator agent proposes a model tailored to the data, while an Inspector agent critically audits each proposal against nine physical constraints and returns it for refinement whenever a violation is detected. We demonstrate this concept with constitutive artificial neural networks (CANNs) and benchmark it on brain tissue, experimental rubber, and synthetic rubber, using two different LLM backbones (Claude Opus 4.7 and Kimi K2.5). Adding the Inspector raises the share of exported models that truly satisfy all physical constraints from 91% to a perfect 100% for Opus and from 37% to 56% for Kimi, while preserving near-baseline accuracy and remarkable generalization to unseen loading paths. In combination, the generated models are physically valid, highly accurate, and extrapolate reliably beyond the training data - properties that together make them directly usable in practice. Separating generation from inspection thus turns LLM-driven constitutive modeling into a genuinely trustworthy process. The paradigm is deliberately technique-agnostic and scales automatically with advances in LLM capability, opening a promising path toward automated, physics-aware model discovery.

</details>


### [138] [Debiased Negative Mining Improves Out-of-distribution Detection with Pre-trained Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23797)
*Bo Peng,Jie Lu,Guangquan Zhang,Zhen Fang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对视觉-语言模型（VLM）进行OOD检测时负标签挖掘存在的“假阴性”偏差问题，提出了一种理论上的去偏挖掘框架，通过蒙特卡洛采样显著提升了OOD检测的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于视觉-语言模型（VLM）的后验OOD检测方法主要依赖启发式规则从无标签语料库中挖掘负标签，但这些方法存在严重的“假阴性”问题，导致模型潜力未能完全发挥。本文旨在解决如何精准挖掘用于OOD评分的真实负标签这一核心挑战。

Method: 该研究通过构建一个理论框架来校正负标签的采样偏差，进而间接逼近负标签的分布。研究表明，这种去偏负样本挖掘可以转化为一种利用ID标签和无标签“野外”语料库数据的蒙特卡洛采样方法。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在多种OOD检测设置下均优于现有基准方法，确立了该领域新的SOTA（当前最佳性能）水平。

Conclusion: 本文提出的去偏负样本挖掘方法不仅在理论上解决了VLM中OOD检测的采样偏差问题，还证明了这种纠偏过程可以自然地转化为基于ID标签和无标签数据的蒙特卡洛采样，为提升OOD检测性能提供了一种高效且稳健的方案。

Abstract: Aiming at identifying unexpected inputs from unknown classes, out-of-distribution (OOD) detection has emerged as a pivotal approach to enhancing the reliability of machine learning models. This paper focuses on the burgeoning paradigm of post-hoc OOD detection with pre-trained vision-language models (VLMs), where a popular pipeline is to detect OOD inputs by examining their affinities between ID labels and negative labels, i.e., those semantically different from ID labels. Due to the unavailability of target OOD labels, existing works predominantly rely on heuristic rules to mine negative labels from unlabeled wild corpus data. Despite the empirical success, we argue that the power of VLM-based OOD detection has yet to be fully unleashed since the notorious false negative problem is far from addressed in the literature. With this motivation, we are interested in addressing the challenge of mining true negative labels for OOD scoring. To this end, we develop a theoretical framework for correcting the sampling bias of negatives labels by indirectly approximating the distribution of negative labels. Perhaps surprisingly, we show that the debiased negative mining can be naturally converted into Monte-Carlo sampling based on ID labels and the unlabeled wild corpus data. Extensive experiments empirically manifest that our method establishes a new state-of-the-art in a variety of OOD detection setups. Code is publicly available at \href{https://github.com/60pen9/Debiased-Negative-Mining-Improves-OOD-Detection-with-Pre-trained-VLMs}{\textcolor{red}{here}}.

</details>


### [139] [Training-Free Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23872)
*Lizhang Chen,Jonathan Li,Chen Liang,Ni Lao,Qiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在推理阶段无需训练即可通过循环利用Transformer中间层来增强模型性能的方法，通过将循环过程建模为ODE的精细化求解，成功提升了多种主流大模型的基准测试表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的循环Transformer方法通常需要端到端的全量训练，成本高昂。研究者希望开发一种能在推理阶段直接增强预训练模型性能的方法，通过复用模型内部组件，在不进行微调或架构修改的情况下提升模型能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为“无训练循环Transformer”的方法。核心在于：1. 在推理阶段，利用轻量级包装器循环执行冻结模型的中间层；2. 并非直接简单的重复应用，而是借鉴常微分方程（ODE）数值求解中前向欧拉法的思想，将大的更新步骤替换为一系列较小的阻尼子步骤（damped sub-steps）进行精细化迭代。

Result: 在包括密集模型、稀疏混合专家（MoE）及MLA+MoE模型在内的七个模型系列中验证了该方法。实验结果显示，Qwen3-4B-Instruct在MMLU-Pro上提升了2.64个百分点，Qwen3-30B-A3B-Instruct在CommonsenseQA上提升了1.14个百分点，Moonlight-16B-A3B-Instruct在OpenBookQA上提升了1.20个百分点。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了无需额外训练即可通过递归应用预训练模型中的中间层来提升模型性能。通过将循环视为对常微分方程（ODE）求解的精细化，该方法提供了一种通用且有效的推理阶段优化手段，显著增强了现有大语言模型在多项基准测试中的表现。

Abstract: We introduce training-free looped transformers, in which a lightweight inference-time wrapper loops a contiguous mid-stack block of layers of a frozen checkpoint without additional fine-tuning, continued training, or architectural changes. Unlike prior looped transformer methods that train with the looped structure end-to-end, we retrofit recurrence onto pretrained models at test time. We show that naive block reapplication usually degrades performance, highlighting the importance of the loop application strategy. Motivated by viewing a pre-norm transformer block as a forward Euler step on an ODE, we instead treat looping as a refinement of the same approximation, replacing one large update with smaller damped sub-steps. Across seven dense, sparse MoE, and MLA+MoE model families, our method improves Qwen3-4B-Instruct by +2.64 pp on MMLU-Pro, Qwen3-30B-A3B-Instruct by +1.14 pp on CommonsenseQA, and Moonlight-16B-A3B-Instruct by +1.20 pp on OpenBookQA.

</details>
